001 # Mobile Design Thinking
002 
003 > **This file prevents AI from using memorized patterns and forces genuine thinking.**
004 > Mechanisms to prevent standard AI training defaults in mobile development.
005 > **The mobile equivalent of frontend's layout decomposition approach.**
006 
007 ---
008 
009 ## üß† DEEP MOBILE THINKING PROTOCOL
010 
011 ### This Process is Mandatory Before Every Mobile Project
012 
013 ```
014 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
015 ‚îÇ                    DEEP MOBILE THINKING                         ‚îÇ
016 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
017 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
018 ‚îÇ  1Ô∏è‚É£ CONTEXT SCAN                                               ‚îÇ
019 ‚îÇ     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ What are my assumptions for this project?               ‚îÇ
020 ‚îÇ         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ QUESTION these assumptions                          ‚îÇ
021 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
022 ‚îÇ  2Ô∏è‚É£ ANTI-DEFAULT ANALYSIS                                      ‚îÇ
023 ‚îÇ     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Am I applying a memorized pattern?                      ‚îÇ
024 ‚îÇ         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Is this pattern REALLY the best for THIS project?   ‚îÇ
025 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
026 ‚îÇ  3Ô∏è‚É£ PLATFORM DECOMPOSITION                                     ‚îÇ
027 ‚îÇ     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Did I think about iOS and Android separately?           ‚îÇ
028 ‚îÇ         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ What are the platform-specific patterns?            ‚îÇ
029 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
030 ‚îÇ  4Ô∏è‚É£ TOUCH INTERACTION BREAKDOWN                                ‚îÇ
031 ‚îÇ     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Did I analyze each interaction individually?            ‚îÇ
032 ‚îÇ         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Did I apply Fitts' Law, Thumb Zone?                 ‚îÇ
033 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
034 ‚îÇ  5Ô∏è‚É£ PERFORMANCE IMPACT ANALYSIS                                ‚îÇ
035 ‚îÇ     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Did I consider performance impact of each component?    ‚îÇ
036 ‚îÇ         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Is the default solution performant?                 ‚îÇ
037 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
038 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
039 ```

043 ## üö´ AI MOBILE DEFAULTS (FORBIDDEN LIST)
044 
045 ### Using These Patterns Automatically is FORBIDDEN!
046 
047 The following patterns are "defaults" that AIs learned from training data.
048 Before using any of these, **QUESTION them and CONSIDER ALTERNATIVES!**
049 
050 ```
051 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
052 ‚îÇ                 üö´ AI MOBILE SAFE HARBOR                        ‚îÇ
053 ‚îÇ           (Default Patterns - Never Use Without Questioning)    ‚îÇ
054 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
055 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
056 ‚îÇ  NAVIGATION DEFAULTS:                                           ‚îÇ
057 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tab bar for every project (Would drawer be better?)        ‚îÇ
058 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Fixed 5 tabs (Are 3 enough? For 6+, drawer?)               ‚îÇ
059 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ "Home" tab on left (What does user behavior say?)          ‚îÇ
060 ‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Hamburger menu (Is it outdated now?)                       ‚îÇ
061 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
062 ‚îÇ  STATE MANAGEMENT DEFAULTS:                                     ‚îÇ
063 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Redux everywhere (Is Zustand/Jotai sufficient?)            ‚îÇ
064 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Global state for everything (Isn't local state enough?)   ‚îÇ
065 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Context Provider hell (Is atom-based better?)              ‚îÇ
066 ‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ BLoC for every Flutter project (Is Riverpod more modern?)  ‚îÇ
067 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
068 ‚îÇ  LIST IMPLEMENTATION DEFAULTS:                                  ‚îÇ
069 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ FlatList as default (Is FlashList more performant?)        ‚îÇ
070 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ windowSize=21 (Is it really needed?)                       ‚îÇ
071 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ removeClippedSubviews (Always?)                            ‚îÇ
072 ‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ListView.builder (Is ListView.separated better?)           ‚îÇ
073 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
074 ‚îÇ  UI PATTERN DEFAULTS:                                           ‚îÇ
075 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ FAB bottom-right (Is bottom-left more accessible?)         ‚îÇ
076 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Pull-to-refresh on every list (Is it needed everywhere?)   ‚îÇ
077 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Swipe-to-delete from left (Is right better?)               ‚îÇ
078 ‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Bottom sheet for every modal (Is full screen better?)      ‚îÇ
079 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
080 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò

085 ## üîç COMPONENT DECOMPOSITION (MANDATORY)
086 
087 ### Decomposition Analysis for Every Screen
088 
089 Before designing any screen, perform this analysis:
090 
091 ```
092 SCREEN: [Screen Name]
093 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ PRIMARY ACTION: [What is the main action?]
094 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Is it in thumb zone? [Yes/No ‚Üí Why?]
095 ‚îÇ
096 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ TOUCH TARGETS: [All tappable elements]
097 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ [Element 1]: [Size]pt ‚Üí Sufficient?
098 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ [Element 2]: [Size]pt ‚Üí Sufficient?
099 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Spacing: [Gap]pt ‚Üí Accidental tap risk?
100 ‚îÇ
101 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SCROLLABLE CONTENT:
102 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Is it a list? ‚Üí FlatList/FlashList [Why this choice?]
103 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Item count: ~[N] ‚Üí Performance consideration?
104 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Fixed height? ‚Üí Is getItemLayout needed?
105 ‚îÇ
106 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ STATE REQUIREMENTS:
107 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Is local state sufficient?
108 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Do I need to lift state?
109 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Is global required? [Why?]
110 ‚îÇ
111 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ PLATFORM DIFFERENCES:
112 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ iOS: [Anything different needed?]
113 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Android: [Anything different needed?]
114 ‚îÇ
115 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ OFFLINE CONSIDERATION:
116 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Should this screen work offline?
117 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Cache strategy: [Yes/No/Which one?]
118 ‚îÇ
119 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ PERFORMANCE IMPACT:
120     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Any heavy components?
121     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Is memoization needed?
122     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Animation performance?
123 ```

125 ---
126 
127 ## üéØ PATTERN QUESTIONING MATRIX
128 
129 Ask these questions for every default pattern:
130 
131 ### Navigation Pattern Questioning
132 
133 | Assumption | Question | Alternative |
134 |------------|----------|-------------|
135 | "I'll use tab bar" | How many destinations? | 3 ‚Üí minimal tabs, 6+ ‚Üí drawer |
136 | "5 tabs" | Are all equally important? | "More" tab? Drawer hybrid? |
137 | "Bottom nav" | iPad/tablet support? | Navigation rail alternative |
138 | "Stack navigation" | Did I consider deep links? | URL structure = navigation structure |
139 
140 ### State Pattern Questioning
141 
142 | Assumption | Question | Alternative |
143 |------------|----------|-------------|
144 | "I'll use Redux" | How complex is the app? | Simple: Zustand, Server: TanStack |
145 | "Global state" | Is this state really global? | Local lift, Context selector |
146 | "Context Provider" | Will re-render be an issue? | Zustand, Jotai (atom-based) |
147 | "BLoC pattern" | Is the boilerplate worth it? | Riverpod (less code) |
148 
149 ### List Pattern Questioning
150 
151 | Assumption | Question | Alternative |
152 |------------|----------|-------------|
153 | "FlatList" | Is performance critical? | FlashList (faster) |
154 | "Standard renderItem" | Is it memoized? | useCallback + React.memo |
155 | "Index key" | Does data order change? | Use item.id |
156 | "ListView" | Are there separators? | ListView.separated |
157 
158 ### UI Pattern Questioning
159 
160 | Assumption | Question | Alternative |
161 |------------|----------|-------------|
162 | "FAB bottom-right" | User handedness? | Accessibility settings |
163 | "Pull-to-refresh" | Does this list need refresh? | Only when necessary |
164 | "Modal bottom sheet" | How much content? | Full screen modal might be better |
165 | "Swipe actions" | Discoverability? | Visible button alternative |
166 
167 ---

169 ## üß™ ANTI-MEMORIZATION TEST
170 
171 ### Ask Yourself Before Every Solution
172 
173 ```
174 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
175 ‚îÇ                    ANTI-MEMORIZATION CHECKLIST                  ‚îÇ
176 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
177 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
178 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Did I pick this solution "because I always do it this way"?  ‚îÇ
179 ‚îÇ    ‚Üí If YES: STOP. Consider alternatives.                       ‚îÇ
180 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
181 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Is this a pattern I've seen frequently in training data?     ‚îÇ
182 ‚îÇ    ‚Üí If YES: Is it REALLY suitable for THIS project?            ‚îÇ
183 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
184 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Did I write this solution automatically without thinking?    ‚îÇ
185 ‚îÇ    ‚Üí If YES: Step back, do decomposition.                       ‚îÇ
186 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
187 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Did I consider an alternative approach?                      ‚îÇ
188 ‚îÇ    ‚Üí If NO: Think of at least 2 alternatives, then decide.      ‚îÇ
189 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
190 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Did I think platform-specifically?                           ‚îÇ
191 ‚îÇ    ‚Üí If NO: Analyze iOS and Android separately.                 ‚îÇ
192 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
193 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Did I consider performance impact of this solution?          ‚îÇ
194 ‚îÇ    ‚Üí If NO: What is the memory, CPU, battery impact?            ‚îÇ
195 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
196 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Is this solution suitable for THIS project's CONTEXT?        ‚îÇ
197 ‚îÇ    ‚Üí If NO: Customize based on context.                         ‚îÇ
198 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
199 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
200 ```

204 ## üìä CONTEXT-BASED DECISION PROTOCOL
205 
206 ### Think Differently Based on Project Type
207 
208 ```
209 DETERMINE PROJECT TYPE:
210         ‚îÇ
211         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ E-Commerce App
212         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation: Tab (Home, Search, Cart, Account)
213         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Lists: Product grids (memoized, image optimized)
214         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance: Image caching CRITICAL
215         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Offline: Cart persistence, product cache
216         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Special: Checkout flow, payment security
217         ‚îÇ
218         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Social/Content App
219         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation: Tab (Feed, Search, Create, Notify, Profile)
220         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Lists: Infinite scroll, complex items
221         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance: Feed rendering CRITICAL
222         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Offline: Feed cache, draft posts
223         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Special: Real-time updates, media handling
224         ‚îÇ
225         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Productivity/SaaS App
226         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation: Drawer or adaptive (mobile tab, tablet rail)
227         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Lists: Data tables, forms
228         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance: Data sync
229         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Offline: Full offline editing
230         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Special: Conflict resolution, background sync
231         ‚îÇ
232         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Utility App
233         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation: Minimal (stack-only possible)
234         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Lists: Probably minimal
235         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance: Fast startup
236         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Offline: Core feature offline
237         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Special: Widget, shortcuts
238         ‚îÇ
239         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Media/Streaming App
240             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation: Tab (Home, Search, Library, Profile)
241             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Lists: Horizontal carousels, vertical feeds
242             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance: Preloading, buffering
243             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Offline: Download management
244             ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Special: Background playback, casting
245 ```

249 ## üîÑ INTERACTION BREAKDOWN
250 
251 ### Analysis for Every Gesture
252 
253 Before adding any gesture:
254 
255 ```
256 GESTURE: [Gesture Type]
257 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ DISCOVERABILITY:
258 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ How will users discover this gesture?
259 ‚îÇ       ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Is there a visual hint?
260 ‚îÇ       ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Will it be shown in onboarding?
261 ‚îÇ       ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Is there a button alternative? (MANDATORY)
262 ‚îÇ
263 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ PLATFORM CONVENTION:
264 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ What does this gesture mean on iOS?
265 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ What does this gesture mean on Android?
266 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Am I deviating from platform convention?
267 ‚îÇ
268 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ ACCESSIBILITY:
269 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Can motor-impaired users perform this gesture?
270 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Is there a VoiceOver/TalkBack alternative?
271 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Does it work with switch control?
272 ‚îÇ
273 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ CONFLICT CHECK:
274 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Does it conflict with system gestures?
275 ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ iOS: Edge swipe back
276 ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Android: Back gesture
277 ‚îÇ   ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Home indicator swipe
278 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Is it consistent with other app gestures?
279 ‚îÇ
280 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ FEEDBACK:
281     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Is haptic feedback defined?
282     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Is visual feedback sufficient?
283     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Is audio feedback needed?
284 ```

288 ## üé≠ SPIRIT OVER CHECKLIST (Mobile Edition)
289 
290 ### Passing the Checklist is Not Enough!
291 
292 | ‚ùå Self-Deception | ‚úÖ Honest Assessment |
293 |-------------------|----------------------|
294 | "Touch target is 44px" (but on edge, unreachable) | "Can user reach it one-handed?" |
295 | "I used FlatList" (but didn't memoize) | "Is scroll smooth?" |
296 | "Platform-specific nav" (but only icons differ) | "Does iOS feel like iOS, Android like Android?" |
297 | "Offline support exists" (but error message is generic) | "What can user actually do offline?" |
298 | "Loading state exists" (but just a spinner) | "Does user know how long to wait?" |
299 
300 > üî¥ **Passing the checklist is NOT the goal. Creating great mobile UX IS the goal.**
301

321    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ iOS: _______________
322    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Android: _______________

328    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ _______________

339 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê

341 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
342 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
343 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Did I complete Component Decomposition?                      ‚îÇ

345 ‚îÇ  ‚ñ° Did I pass the Anti-Memorization Test?                       ‚îÇ

350 ‚îÇ  ‚ö†Ô∏è Do not write code without completing these!                 ‚îÇ
351 ‚îÇ                                                                 ‚îÇ
352 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
353 ```
354 
355 ---
356 
357 > **Remember:** If you chose a solution "because that's how it's always done," you chose WITHOUT THINKING. Every project is unique. Every context is different. Every user behavior is specific. **THINK, then code.**
=== FILE_CAPSULE_END FID:F105 ===

=== FILE_CAPSULE_BEGIN FID:F106 path:skills/mobile-design/mobile-navigation.md hash:1d9aefcd45146bc39aa4ac12b27e89343cc1f206ea2dafa41269e72433930711 lines:458 ===
001 # Mobile Navigation Reference
002 
003 > Navigation patterns, deep linking, back handling, and tab/stack/drawer decisions.
004 > **Navigation is the skeleton of your app‚Äîget it wrong and everything feels broken.**
005 
006 ---
007 
008 ## 1. Navigation Selection Decision Tree
009 
010 ```
011 WHAT TYPE OF APP?
012         ‚îÇ
013         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 3-5 top-level sections (equal importance)
014         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ Tab Bar / Bottom Navigation
015         ‚îÇ       Examples: Social, E-commerce, Utility
016         ‚îÇ
017         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Deep hierarchical content (drill down)
018         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ Stack Navigation
019         ‚îÇ       Examples: Settings, Email folders
020         ‚îÇ
021         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Many destinations (>5 top-level)
022         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ Drawer Navigation
023         ‚îÇ       Examples: Gmail, complex enterprise
024         ‚îÇ
025         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Single linear flow
026         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ Stack only (wizard/onboarding)
027         ‚îÇ       Examples: Checkout, Setup flow
028         ‚îÇ
029         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Tablet/Foldable
030             ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ Navigation Rail + List-Detail
031                 Examples: Mail, Notes on iPad
032 ```
033 
034 ---
035 
036 ## 2. Tab Bar Navigation
037 
038 ### When to Use
039 
040 ```
041 ‚úÖ USE Tab Bar when:
042 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 3-5 top-level destinations
043 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Destinations are of equal importance
044 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User frequently switches between them
045 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Each tab has independent navigation stack
046 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ App is used in short sessions
047 
048 ‚ùå AVOID Tab Bar when:
049 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ More than 5 destinations
050 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Destinations have clear hierarchy
051 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tabs would be used very unequally
052 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Content flows in a sequence
053 ```
054 
055 ### Tab Bar Best Practices
056 
057 ```
058 iOS Tab Bar:
059 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Height: 49pt (83pt with home indicator)
060 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Max items: 5
061 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons: SF Symbols, 25√ó25pt
062 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Labels: Always show (accessibility)
063 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Active indicator: Tint color
064 
065 Android Bottom Navigation:
066 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Height: 80dp
067 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Max items: 5 (3-5 ideal)
068 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons: Material Symbols, 24dp
069 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Labels: Always show
070 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Active indicator: Pill shape + filled icon
071 ```
072 
073 ### Tab State Preservation
074 
075 ```
076 RULE: Each tab maintains its own navigation stack.
077 
078 User journey:
079 1. Home tab ‚Üí Drill into item ‚Üí Add to cart
080 2. Switch to Profile tab
081 3. Switch back to Home tab
082 ‚Üí Should return to "Add to cart" screen, NOT home root
083 
084 Implementation:
085 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ React Navigation: Each tab has own navigator
086 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Flutter: IndexedStack for state preservation
087 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Never reset tab stack on switch
088 ```
089 
090 ---
091 
092 ## 3. Stack Navigation
093 
094 ### Core Concepts
095 
096 ```
097 Stack metaphor: Cards stacked on top of each other
098 
099 Push: Add screen on top
100 Pop: Remove top screen (back)
101 Replace: Swap current screen
102 Reset: Clear stack, set new root
103 
104 Visual: New screen slides in from right (LTR)
105 Back: Screen slides out to right
106 ```
107 
108 ### Stack Navigation Patterns
109 
110 | Pattern | Use Case | Implementation |
111 |---------|----------|----------------|
112 | **Simple Stack** | Linear flow | Push each step |
113 | **Nested Stack** | Sections with sub-navigation | Stack inside tab |
114 | **Modal Stack** | Focused tasks | Present modally |
115 | **Auth Stack** | Login vs Main | Conditional root |
116 
117 ### Back Button Handling
118 
119 ```
120 iOS:
121 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Edge swipe from left (system)
122 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Back button in nav bar (optional)
123 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Interactive pop gesture
124 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Never override swipe back without good reason
125 
126 Android:
127 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ System back button/gesture
128 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Up button in toolbar (optional, for drill-down)
129 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Predictive back animation (Android 14+)
130 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Must handle back correctly (Activity/Fragment)
131 
132 Cross-Platform Rule:
133 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Back ALWAYS navigates up the stack
134 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Never hijack back for other purposes
135 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Confirm before discarding unsaved data
136 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Deep links should allow full back traversal
137 ```
138 
139 ---
140 
141 ## 4. Drawer Navigation
142 
143 ### When to Use
144 
145 ```
146 ‚úÖ USE Drawer when:
147 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ More than 5 top-level destinations
148 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Less frequently accessed destinations
149 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Complex app with many features
150 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Need for branding/user info in nav
151 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Tablet/large screen with persistent drawer
152 
153 ‚ùå AVOID Drawer when:
154 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 5 or fewer destinations (use tabs)
155 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ All destinations equally important
156 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Mobile-first simple app
157 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Discoverability is critical (drawer is hidden)
158 ```
159 
160 ### Drawer Patterns
161 
162 ```
163 Modal Drawer:
164 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Opens over content (scrim behind)
165 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Swipe to open from edge
166 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Hamburger icon ( ‚ò∞ ) triggers
167 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Most common on mobile
168 
169 Permanent Drawer:
170 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Always visible (large screens)
171 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Content shifts over
172 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Good for productivity apps
173 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Tablets, desktops
174 
175 Navigation Rail (Android):
176 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Narrow vertical strip
177 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons + optional labels
178 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ For tablets in portrait
179 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 80dp width
180 ```
181 
182 ---
183 
184 ## 5. Modal Navigation
185 
186 ### Modal vs Push
187 
188 ```
189 PUSH (Stack):                    MODAL:
190 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Horizontal slide             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Vertical slide up (sheet)
191 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Part of hierarchy            ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Separate task
192 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Back returns                 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dismiss (X) returns
193 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Same navigation context      ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Own navigation context
194 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ "Drill in"                   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ "Focus on task"
195 
196 USE MODAL for:
197 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Creating new content
198 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Settings/preferences
199 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Completing a transaction
200 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Self-contained workflows
201 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Quick actions
202 ```
203 
204 ### Modal Types
205 
206 | Type | iOS | Android | Use Case |
207 |------|-----|---------|----------|
208 | **Sheet** | `.sheet` | Bottom Sheet | Quick tasks |
209 | **Full Screen** | `.fullScreenCover` | Full Activity | Complex forms |
210 | **Alert** | Alert | Dialog | Confirmations |
211 | **Action Sheet** | Action Sheet | Menu/Bottom Sheet | Choose from options |
212 
213 ### Modal Dismissal
214 
215 ```
216 Users expect to dismiss modals by:
217 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tapping X / Close button
218 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Swiping down (sheet)
219 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tapping scrim (non-critical)
220 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ System back (Android)
221 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Hardware back (old Android)
222 
223 RULE: Only block dismissal for unsaved data.
224 ```
225 
226 ---
227 
228 ## 6. Deep Linking
229 
230 ### Why Deep Links from Day One
231 
232 ```
233 Deep links enable:
234 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Push notification navigation
235 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Sharing content
236 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Marketing campaigns
237 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Spotlight/Search integration
238 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Widget navigation
239 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ External app integration
240 
241 Building later is HARD:
242 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Requires navigation refactor
243 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Screen dependencies unclear
244 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Parameter passing complex
245 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Always plan deep links at start
246 ```
247 
248 ### URL Structure
249 
250 ```
251 Scheme://host/path?params
252 
253 Examples:
254 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ myapp://product/123
255 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ https://myapp.com/product/123 (Universal/App Link)
256 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ myapp://checkout?promo=SAVE20
257 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ myapp://tab/profile/settings
258 
259 Hierarchy should match navigation:
260 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ myapp://home
261 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ myapp://home/product/123
262 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ myapp://home/product/123/reviews
263 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ URL path = navigation path
264 ```
265 
266 ### Deep Link Navigation Rules
267 
268 ```
269 1. FULL STACK CONSTRUCTION
270    Deep link to myapp://product/123 should:
271    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Put Home at root of stack
272    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Push Product screen on top
273    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Back button returns to Home
274 
275 2. AUTHENTICATION AWARENESS
276    If deep link requires auth:
277    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Save intended destination
278    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Redirect to login
279    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ After login, navigate to destination
280 
281 3. INVALID LINKS
282    If deep link target doesn't exist:
283    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigate to fallback (home)
284    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Show error message
285    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Never crash or blank screen
286 
287 4. STATEFUL NAVIGATION
288    Deep link during active session:
289    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Don't blow away current stack
290    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Push on top OR
291    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Ask user if should navigate away
292 ```
293 
294 ---
295 
296 ## 7. Navigation State Persistence
297 
298 ### What to Persist
299 
300 ```
301 SHOULD persist:
302 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Current tab selection
303 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Scroll position in lists
304 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Form draft data
305 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Recent navigation stack
306 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ User preferences
307 
308 SHOULD NOT persist:
309 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Modal states (dialogs)
310 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Temporary UI states
311 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Stale data (refresh on return)
312 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Authentication state (use secure storage)
313 ```
314 
315 ### Implementation
316 
317 ```javascript
318 // React Navigation - State Persistence
319 const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
320 const [initialState, setInitialState] = useState();
321 
322 useEffect(() => {
323   const loadState = async () => {
324     const savedState = await AsyncStorage.getItem('NAV_STATE');
325     if (savedState) setInitialState(JSON.parse(savedState));
326     setIsReady(true);
327   };
328   loadState();
329 }, []);
330 
331 const handleStateChange = (state) => {
332   AsyncStorage.setItem('NAV_STATE', JSON.stringify(state));
333 };
334 
335 <NavigationContainer
336   initialState={initialState}
337   onStateChange={handleStateChange}
338 >
339 ```
340 
341 ---
342 
343 ## 8. Transition Animations
344 
345 ### Platform Defaults
346 
347 ```
348 iOS Transitions:
349 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Push: Slide from right
350 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Modal: Slide from bottom (sheet) or fade
351 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tab switch: Cross-fade
352 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Interactive: Swipe to go back
353 
354 Android Transitions:
355 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Push: Fade + slide from right
356 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Modal: Slide from bottom
357 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tab switch: Cross-fade or none
358 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Shared element: Hero animations
359 ```
360 
361 ### Custom Transitions
362 
363 ```
364 When to custom:
365 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Brand identity requires it
366 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Shared element connections
367 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Special reveal effects
368 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Keep it subtle, <300ms
369 
370 When to use default:
371 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Most of the time
372 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Standard drill-down
373 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Platform consistency
374 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance critical paths
375 ```
376 
377 ### Shared Element Transitions
378 
379 ```
380 Connect elements between screens:
381 
382 Screen A: Product card with image
383             ‚Üì (tap)
384 Screen B: Product detail with same image (expanded)
385 
386 Image animates from card position to detail position.
387 
388 Implementation:
389 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ React Navigation: shared element library
390 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Flutter: Hero widget
391 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SwiftUI: matchedGeometryEffect
392 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Compose: Shared element transitions
393 ```
394 
395 ---
396 
397 ## 9. Navigation Anti-Patterns
398 
399 ### ‚ùå Navigation Sins
400 
401 | Anti-Pattern | Problem | Solution |
402 |--------------|---------|----------|
403 | **Inconsistent back** | User confused, can't predict | Always pop stack |
404 | **Hidden navigation** | Features undiscoverable | Visible tabs/drawer trigger |
405 | **Deep nesting** | User gets lost | Max 3-4 levels, breadcrumbs |
406 | **Breaking swipe back** | iOS users frustrated | Never override gesture |
407 | **No deep links** | Can't share, bad notifications | Plan from start |
408 | **Tab stack reset** | Work lost on switch | Preserve tab states |
409 | **Modal for primary flow** | Can't back track | Use stack navigation |
410 
411 ### ‚ùå AI Navigation Mistakes
412 
413 ```
414 AI tends to:
415 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use modals for everything (wrong)
416 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Forget tab state preservation (wrong)
417 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Skip deep linking (wrong)
418 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Override platform back behavior (wrong)
419 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reset stack on tab switch (wrong)
420 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Ignore predictive back (Android 14+)
421 
422 RULE: Use platform navigation patterns.
423 Don't reinvent navigation.
424 ```
425 
426 ---
427 
428 ## 10. Navigation Checklist
429 
430 ### Before Navigation Architecture
431 
432 - [ ] App type determined (tabs/drawer/stack)
433 - [ ] Number of top-level destinations counted
434 - [ ] Deep link URL scheme planned
435 - [ ] Auth flow integrated with navigation
436 - [ ] Tablet/large screen considered
437 
438 ### Before Every Screen
439 
440 - [ ] Can user navigate back? (not dead end)
441 - [ ] Deep link to this screen planned
442 - [ ] State preserved on navigate away/back
443 - [ ] Transition appropriate for relationship
444 - [ ] Auth required? Handled?
445 
446 ### Before Release
447 
448 - [ ] All deep links tested
449 - [ ] Back button works everywhere
450 - [ ] Tab states preserved correctly
451 - [ ] Edge swipe back works (iOS)
452 - [ ] Predictive back works (Android 14+)
453 - [ ] Universal/App links configured
454 - [ ] Push notification deep links work
455 
456 ---
457 
458 > **Remember:** Navigation is invisible when done right. Users shouldn't think about HOW to get somewhere‚Äîthey just get there. If they notice navigation, something is wrong.

=== FILE_CAPSULE_BEGIN FID:F107 path:skills/mobile-design/mobile-performance.md hash:1acdf49acba81035b6e11870b5e2b80e2b585178f6b524065c6937fb42da7059 lines:767 ===
001 # Mobile Performance Reference
002 
003 > Deep dive into React Native and Flutter performance optimization, 60fps animations, memory management, and battery considerations.
004 > **This file covers the #1 area where AI-generated code FAILS.**
005 
006 ---
007 
008 ## 1. The Mobile Performance Mindset
009 
010 ### Why Mobile Performance is Different
011 
012 ```
013 DESKTOP:                          MOBILE:
014 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Unlimited power               ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Battery matters
015 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Abundant RAM                  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ RAM is shared, limited
016 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Stable network                ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Network is unreliable
017 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ CPU always available          ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ CPU throttles when hot
018 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ User expects fast anyway      ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ User expects INSTANT
019 ```
020 
021 ### Performance Budget Concept
022 
023 ```
024 Every frame must complete in:
025 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 60fps ‚Üí 16.67ms per frame
026 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 120fps (ProMotion) ‚Üí 8.33ms per frame
027 
028 If your code takes longer:
029 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Frame drops ‚Üí Janky scroll/animation
030 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User perceives as "slow" or "broken"
031 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ They WILL uninstall your app
032 ```
033 
034 ---
035 
036 ## 2. React Native Performance
037 
038 ### üö´ The #1 AI Mistake: ScrollView for Lists
039 
040 ```javascript
041 // ‚ùå NEVER DO THIS - AI's favorite mistake
042 <ScrollView>
043   {items.map(item => (
044     <ItemComponent key={item.id} item={item} />
045   ))}
046 </ScrollView>
047 
048 // Why it's catastrophic:
049 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Renders ALL items immediately (1000 items = 1000 renders)
050 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Memory explodes
051 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Initial render takes seconds
052 // ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Scroll becomes janky
053 
054 // ‚úÖ ALWAYS USE FlatList
055 <FlatList
056   data={items}
057   renderItem={renderItem}
058   keyExtractor={item => item.id}
059 />
060 ```
061 
062 ### FlatList Optimization Checklist
063 
064 ```javascript
065 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: All optimizations applied
066 
067 // 1. Memoize the item component
068 const ListItem = React.memo(({ item }: { item: Item }) => {
069   return (
070     <Pressable style={styles.item}>
071       <Text>{item.title}</Text>
072     </Pressable>
073   );
074 });
075 
076 // 2. Memoize renderItem with useCallback
077 const renderItem = useCallback(
078   ({ item }: { item: Item }) => <ListItem item={item} />,
079   [] // Empty deps = never recreated
080 );
081 
082 // 3. Stable keyExtractor (NEVER use index!)
083 const keyExtractor = useCallback((item: Item) => item.id, []);
084 
085 // 4. Provide getItemLayout for fixed-height items
086 const getItemLayout = useCallback(
087   (data: Item[] | null, index: number) => ({
088     length: ITEM_HEIGHT, // Fixed height
089     offset: ITEM_HEIGHT * index,
090     index,
091   }),
092   []
093 );
094 
095 // 5. Apply to FlatList
096 <FlatList
097   data={items}
098   renderItem={renderItem}
099   keyExtractor={keyExtractor}
100   getItemLayout={getItemLayout}
101   // Performance props
102   removeClippedSubviews={true} // Android: detach off-screen
103   maxToRenderPerBatch={10} // Items per batch
104   windowSize={5} // Render window (5 = 2 screens each side)
105   initialNumToRender={10} // Initial items
106   updateCellsBatchingPeriod={50} // Batching delay
107 />
108 ```
109 
110 ### Why Each Optimization Matters
111 
112 | Optimization | What It Prevents | Impact |
113 |--------------|------------------|--------|
114 | `React.memo` | Re-render on parent change | üî¥ Critical |
115 | `useCallback renderItem` | New function every render | üî¥ Critical |
116 | Stable `keyExtractor` | Wrong item recycling | üî¥ Critical |
117 | `getItemLayout` | Async layout calculation | üü° High |
118 | `removeClippedSubviews` | Memory from off-screen | üü° High |
119 | `maxToRenderPerBatch` | Blocking main thread | üü¢ Medium |
120 | `windowSize` | Memory usage | üü¢ Medium |
121 
122 ### FlashList: The Better Option
123 
124 ```javascript
125 // Consider FlashList for better performance
126 import { FlashList } from "@shopify/flash-list";
127 
128 <FlashList
129   data={items}
130   renderItem={renderItem}
131   estimatedItemSize={ITEM_HEIGHT}
132   keyExtractor={keyExtractor}
133 />
134 
135 // Benefits over FlatList:
136 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Faster recycling
137 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Better memory management
138 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Simpler API
139 // ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Fewer optimization props needed
140 ```
141 
142 ### Animation Performance
143 
144 ```javascript
145 // ‚ùå JS-driven animation (blocks JS thread)
146 Animated.timing(value, {
147   toValue: 1,
148   duration: 300,
149   useNativeDriver: false, // BAD!
150 }).start();
151 
152 // ‚úÖ Native-driver animation (runs on UI thread)
153 Animated.timing(value, {
154   toValue: 1,
155   duration: 300,
156   useNativeDriver: true, // GOOD!
157 }).start();
158 
159 // Native driver supports ONLY:
160 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ transform (translate, scale, rotate)
161 // ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ opacity
162 //
163 // Does NOT support:
164 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ width, height
165 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ backgroundColor
166 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ borderRadius changes
167 // ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ margin, padding
168 ```
169 
170 ### Reanimated for Complex Animations
171 
172 ```javascript
173 // For animations native driver can't handle, use Reanimated 3
174 
175 import Animated, {
176   useSharedValue,
177   useAnimatedStyle,
178   withSpring,
179 } from 'react-native-reanimated';
180 
181 const Component = () => {
182   const offset = useSharedValue(0);
183 
184   const animatedStyles = useAnimatedStyle(() => ({
185     transform: [{ translateX: withSpring(offset.value) }],
186   }));
187 
188   return <Animated.View style={animatedStyles} />;
189 };
190 
191 // Benefits:
192 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Runs on UI thread (60fps guaranteed)
193 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Can animate any property
194 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Gesture-driven animations
195 // ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Worklets for complex logic
196 ```
197 
198 ### Memory Leak Prevention
199 
200 ```javascript
201 // ‚ùå Memory leak: uncleared interval
202 useEffect(() => {
203   const interval = setInterval(() => {
204     fetchData();
205   }, 5000);
206   // Missing cleanup!
207 }, []);
208 
209 // ‚úÖ Proper cleanup
210 useEffect(() => {
211   const interval = setInterval(() => {
212     fetchData();
213   }, 5000);
214 
215   return () => clearInterval(interval); // CLEANUP!
216 }, []);
217 
218 // Common memory leak sources:
219 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Timers (setInterval, setTimeout)
220 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Event listeners
221 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Subscriptions (WebSocket, PubSub)
222 // ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Async operations that update state after unmount
223 // ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Image caching without limits
224 ```
225 
226 ### React Native Performance Checklist
227 
228 ```markdown
229 ## Before Every List
230 - [ ] Using FlatList or FlashList (NOT ScrollView)
231 - [ ] renderItem is useCallback memoized
232 - [ ] List items are React.memo wrapped
233 - [ ] keyExtractor uses stable ID (NOT index)
234 - [ ] getItemLayout provided (if fixed height)
235 
236 ## Before Every Animation
237 - [ ] useNativeDriver: true (if possible)
238 - [ ] Using Reanimated for complex animations
239 - [ ] Only animating transform/opacity
240 - [ ] Tested on low-end Android device
241 
242 ## Before Any Release
243 - [ ] console.log statements removed
244 - [ ] Cleanup functions in all useEffects
245 - [ ] No memory leaks (test with profiler)
246 - [ ] Tested in release build (not dev)
247 ```
248 
249 ---
250 
251 ## 3. Flutter Performance
252 
253 ### üö´ The #1 AI Mistake: setState Overuse
254 
255 ```dart
256 // ‚ùå WRONG: setState rebuilds ENTIRE widget tree
257 class BadCounter extends StatefulWidget {
258   @override
259   State<BadCounter> createState() => _BadCounterState();
260 }
261 
262 class _BadCounterState extends State<BadCounter> {
263   int _counter = 0;
264 
265   void _increment() {
266     setState(() {
267       _counter++; // This rebuilds EVERYTHING below!
268     });
269   }
270 
271   @override
272   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
273     return Column(
274       children: [
275         Text('Counter: $_counter'),
276         ExpensiveWidget(), // Rebuilds unnecessarily!
277         AnotherExpensiveWidget(), // Rebuilds unnecessarily!
278       ],
279     );
280   }
281 }
282 ```
283 
284 ### The `const` Constructor Revolution
285 
286 ```dart
287 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: const prevents rebuilds
288 
289 class GoodCounter extends StatefulWidget {
290   const GoodCounter({super.key}); // CONST constructor!
291 
292   @override
293   State<GoodCounter> createState() => _GoodCounterState();
294 }
295 
296 class _GoodCounterState extends State<GoodCounter> {
297   int _counter = 0;
298 
299   @override
300   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
301     return Column(
302       children: [
303         Text('Counter: $_counter'),
304         const ExpensiveWidget(), // Won't rebuild!
305         const AnotherExpensiveWidget(), // Won't rebuild!
306       ],
307     );
308   }
309 }
310 
311 // RULE: Add `const` to EVERY widget that doesn't depend on state
312 ```
313 
314 ### Targeted State Management
315 
316 ```dart
317 // ‚ùå setState rebuilds whole tree
318 setState(() => _value = newValue);
319 
320 // ‚úÖ ValueListenableBuilder: surgical rebuilds
321 class TargetedState extends StatelessWidget {
322   final ValueNotifier<int> counter = ValueNotifier(0);
323 
324   @override
325   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
326     return Column(
327       children: [
328         // Only this rebuilds when counter changes
329         ValueListenableBuilder<int>(
330           valueListenable: counter,
331           builder: (context, value, child) => Text('$value'),
332           child: const Icon(Icons.star), // Won't rebuild!
333         ),
334         const ExpensiveWidget(), // Never rebuilds
335       ],
336     );
337   }
338 }
339 ```
340 
341 ### Riverpod/Provider Best Practices
342 
343 ```dart
344 // ‚ùå WRONG: Reading entire provider in build
345 Widget build(BuildContext context) {
346   final state = ref.watch(myProvider); // Rebuilds on ANY change
347   return Text(state.name);
348 }
349 
350 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: Select only what you need
351 Widget build(BuildContext context) {
352   final name = ref.watch(myProvider.select((s) => s.name));
353   return Text(name); // Only rebuilds when name changes
354 }
355 ```
356 
357 ### ListView Optimization
358 
359 ```dart
360 // ‚ùå WRONG: ListView without builder (renders all)
361 ListView(
362   children: items.map((item) => ItemWidget(item)).toList(),
363 )
364 
365 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: ListView.builder (lazy rendering)
366 ListView.builder(
367   itemCount: items.length,
368   itemBuilder: (context, index) => ItemWidget(items[index]),
369   // Additional optimizations:
370   itemExtent: 56, // Fixed height = faster layout
371   cacheExtent: 100, // Pre-render distance
372 )
373 
374 // ‚úÖ EVEN BETTER: ListView.separated for dividers
375 ListView.separated(
376   itemCount: items.length,
377   itemBuilder: (context, index) => ItemWidget(items[index]),
378   separatorBuilder: (context, index) => const Divider(),
379 )
380 ```
381 
382 ### Image Optimization
383 
384 ```dart
385 // ‚ùå WRONG: No caching, full resolution
386 Image.network(url)
387 
388 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: Cached with proper sizing
389 CachedNetworkImage(
390   imageUrl: url,
391   width: 100,
392   height: 100,
393   fit: BoxFit.cover,
394   memCacheWidth: 200, // Cache at 2x for retina
395   memCacheHeight: 200,
396   placeholder: (context, url) => const Skeleton(),
397   errorWidget: (context, url, error) => const Icon(Icons.error),
398 )
399 ```
400 
401 ### Dispose Pattern
402 
403 ```dart
404 class MyWidget extends StatefulWidget {
405   @override
406   State<MyWidget> createState() => _MyWidgetState();
407 }
408 
409 class _MyWidgetState extends State<MyWidget> {
410   late final StreamSubscription _subscription;
411   late final AnimationController _controller;
412   late final TextEditingController _textController;
413 
414   @override
415   void initState() {
416     super.initState();
417     _subscription = stream.listen((_) {});
418     _controller = AnimationController(vsync: this);
419     _textController = TextEditingController();
420   }
421 
422   @override
423   void dispose() {
424     // ALWAYS dispose in reverse order of creation
425     _textController.dispose();
426     _controller.dispose();
427     _subscription.cancel();
428     super.dispose();
429   }
430 
431   @override
432   Widget build(BuildContext context) => Container();
433 }
434 ```
435 
436 ### Flutter Performance Checklist
437 
438 ```markdown
439 ## Before Every Widget
440 - [ ] const constructor added (if no runtime args)
441 - [ ] const keywords on static children
442 - [ ] Minimal setState scope
443 - [ ] Using selectors for provider watches
444 
445 ## Before Every List
446 - [ ] Using ListView.builder (NOT ListView with children)
447 - [ ] itemExtent provided (if fixed height)
448 - [ ] Image caching with size limits
449 
450 ## Before Any Animation
451 - [ ] Using Impeller (Flutter 3.16+)
452 - [ ] Avoiding Opacity widget (use FadeTransition)
453 - [ ] TickerProviderStateMixin for AnimationController
454 
455 ## Before Any Release
456 - [ ] All dispose() methods implemented
457 - [ ] No print() in production
458 - [ ] Tested in profile/release mode
459 - [ ] DevTools performance overlay checked
460 ```
461 
462 ---
463 
464 ## 4. Animation Performance (Both Platforms)
465 
466 ### The 60fps Imperative
467 
468 ```
469 Human eye detects:
470 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ < 24 fps ‚Üí "Slideshow" (broken)
471 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 24-30 fps ‚Üí "Choppy" (uncomfortable)
472 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 30-45 fps ‚Üí "Noticeably not smooth"
473 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 45-60 fps ‚Üí "Smooth" (acceptable)
474 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 60 fps ‚Üí "Buttery" (target)
475 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 120 fps ‚Üí "Premium" (ProMotion devices)
476 
477 NEVER ship < 60fps animations.
478 ```
479 
480 ### GPU vs CPU Animation
481 
482 ```
483 GPU-ACCELERATED (FAST):          CPU-BOUND (SLOW):
484 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ transform: translate          ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ width, height
485 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ transform: scale              ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ top, left, right, bottom
486 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ transform: rotate             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ margin, padding
487 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ opacity                       ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ border-radius (animated)
488 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ (Composited, off main)        ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ box-shadow (animated)
489 
490 RULE: Only animate transform and opacity.
491 Everything else causes layout recalculation.
492 ```
493 
494 ### Animation Timing Guide
495 
496 | Animation Type | Duration | Easing |
497 |----------------|----------|--------|
498 | Micro-interaction | 100-200ms | ease-out |
499 | Standard transition | 200-300ms | ease-out |
500 | Page transition | 300-400ms | ease-in-out |
501 | Complex/dramatic | 400-600ms | ease-in-out |
502 | Loading skeletons | 1000-1500ms | linear (loop) |
503 
504 ### Spring Physics
505 
506 ```javascript
507 // React Native Reanimated
508 withSpring(targetValue, {
509   damping: 15,      // How quickly it settles (higher = faster stop)
510   stiffness: 150,   // How "tight" the spring (higher = faster)
511   mass: 1,          // Weight of the object
512 })
513 
514 // Flutter
515 SpringSimulation(
516   SpringDescription(
517     mass: 1,
518     stiffness: 150,
519     damping: 15,
520   ),
521   start,
522   end,
523   velocity,
524 )
525 
526 // Natural feel ranges:
527 // Damping: 10-20 (bouncy to settled)
528 // Stiffness: 100-200 (loose to tight)
529 // Mass: 0.5-2 (light to heavy)
530 ```
531 
532 ---
533 
534 ## 5. Memory Management
535 
536 ### Common Memory Leaks
537 
538 | Source | Platform | Solution |
539 |--------|----------|----------|
540 | Timers | Both | Clear in cleanup/dispose |
541 | Event listeners | Both | Remove in cleanup/dispose |
542 | Subscriptions | Both | Cancel in cleanup/dispose |
543 | Large images | Both | Limit cache, resize |
544 | Async after unmount | RN | isMounted check or AbortController |
545 | Animation controllers | Flutter | Dispose controllers |
546 
547 ### Image Memory
548 
549 ```
550 Image memory = width √ó height √ó 4 bytes (RGBA)
551 
552 1080p image = 1920 √ó 1080 √ó 4 = 8.3 MB
553 4K image = 3840 √ó 2160 √ó 4 = 33.2 MB
554 
555 10 4K images = 332 MB ‚Üí App crash!
556 
557 RULE: Always resize images to display size (or 2-3x for retina).
558 ```
559 
560 ### Memory Profiling
561 
562 ```
563 React Native:
564 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Flipper ‚Üí Memory tab
565 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Xcode Instruments (iOS)
566 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Android Studio Profiler
567 
568 Flutter:
569 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ DevTools ‚Üí Memory tab
570 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Observatory
571 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ flutter run --profile
572 ```
573 
574 ---
575 
576 ## 6. Battery Optimization
577 
578 ### Battery Drain Sources
579 
580 | Source | Impact | Mitigation |
581 |--------|--------|------------|
582 | **Screen on** | üî¥ Highest | Dark mode on OLED |
583 | **GPS continuous** | üî¥ Very high | Use significant change |
584 | **Network requests** | üü° High | Batch, cache aggressively |
585 | **Animations** | üü° Medium | Reduce when low battery |
586 | **Background work** | üü° Medium | Defer non-critical |
587 | **CPU computation** | üü¢ Lower | Offload to backend |
588 
589 ### OLED Battery Saving
590 
591 ```
592 OLED screens: Black pixels = OFF = 0 power
593 
594 Dark mode savings:
595 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ True black (#000000) ‚Üí Maximum savings
596 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dark gray (#1a1a1a) ‚Üí Slight savings
597 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Any color ‚Üí Some power
598 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ White (#FFFFFF) ‚Üí Maximum power
599 
600 RULE: On dark mode, use true black for backgrounds.
601 ```
602 
603 ### Background Task Guidelines
604 
605 ```
606 iOS:
607 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Background refresh: Limited, system-scheduled
608 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Push notifications: Use for important updates
609 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Background modes: Location, audio, VoIP only
610 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Background tasks: Max ~30 seconds
611 
612 Android:
613 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ WorkManager: System-scheduled, battery-aware
614 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Foreground service: Visible to user, continuous
615 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ JobScheduler: Batch network operations
616 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Doze mode: Respect it, batch operations
617 ```
618 
619 ---
620 
621 ## 7. Network Performance
622 
623 ### Offline-First Architecture
624 
625 ```
626                     ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
627                     ‚îÇ     UI       ‚îÇ
628                     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
629                            ‚îÇ
630                     ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚ñº‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
631                     ‚îÇ   Cache      ‚îÇ ‚Üê Read from cache FIRST
632                     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
633                            ‚îÇ
634                     ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚ñº‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
635                     ‚îÇ   Network    ‚îÇ ‚Üê Update cache from network
636                     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
637 
638 Benefits:
639 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Instant UI (no loading spinner for cached data)
640 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Works offline
641 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reduces data usage
642 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Better UX on slow networks
643 ```
644 
645 ### Request Optimization
646 
647 ```
648 BATCH: Combine multiple requests into one
649 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 10 small requests ‚Üí 1 batch request
650 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reduces connection overhead
651 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Better for battery (radio on once)
652 
653 CACHE: Don't re-fetch unchanged data
654 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ ETag/If-None-Match headers
655 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Cache-Control headers
656 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Stale-while-revalidate pattern
657 
658 COMPRESS: Reduce payload size
659 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ gzip/brotli compression
660 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Request only needed fields (GraphQL)
661 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Paginate large lists
662 ```
663 
664 ---
665 
666 ## 8. Performance Testing
667 
668 ### What to Test
669 
670 | Metric | Target | Tool |
671 |--------|--------|------|
672 | **Frame rate** | ‚â• 60fps | Performance overlay |
673 | **Memory** | Stable, no growth | Profiler |
674 | **Cold start** | < 2s | Manual timing |
675 | **TTI (Time to Interactive)** | < 3s | Lighthouse |
676 | **List scroll** | No jank | Manual feel |
677 | **Animation smoothness** | No drops | Performance monitor |
678 
679 ### Test on Real Devices
680 
681 ```
682 ‚ö†Ô∏è NEVER trust only:
683 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Simulator/emulator (faster than real)
684 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dev mode (slower than release)
685 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ High-end devices only
686 
687 ‚úÖ ALWAYS test on:
688 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Low-end Android (< $200 phone)
689 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Older iOS device (iPhone 8 or SE)
690 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Release/profile build
691 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ With real data (not 10 items)
692 ```
693 
694 ### Performance Monitoring Checklist
695 
696 ```markdown
697 ## During Development
698 - [ ] Performance overlay enabled
699 - [ ] Watching for dropped frames
700 - [ ] Memory usage stable
701 - [ ] No console warnings about performance
702 
703 ## Before Release
704 - [ ] Tested on low-end device
705 - [ ] Profiled memory over extended use
706 - [ ] Cold start time measured
707 - [ ] List scroll tested with 1000+ items
708 - [ ] Animations tested at 60fps
709 - [ ] Network tested on slow 3G
710 ```

714 ## 9. Quick Reference Card
715 
716 ### React Native Essentials
717 
718 ```javascript
719 // List: Always use
720 <FlatList
721   data={data}
722   renderItem={useCallback(({item}) => <MemoItem item={item} />, [])}
723   keyExtractor={useCallback(item => item.id, [])}
724   getItemLayout={useCallback((_, i) => ({length: H, offset: H*i, index: i}), [])}
725 />
726 
727 // Animation: Always native
728 useNativeDriver: true
729 
730 // Cleanup: Always present
731 useEffect(() => {
732   return () => cleanup();
733 }, []);
734 ```
735 
736 ### Flutter Essentials
737 
738 ```dart
739 // Widgets: Always const
740 const MyWidget()
741 
742 // Lists: Always builder
743 ListView.builder(itemBuilder: ...)
744 
745 // State: Always targeted
746 ValueListenableBuilder() or ref.watch(provider.select(...))
747 
748 // Dispose: Always cleanup
749 @override
750 void dispose() {
751   controller.dispose();
752   super.dispose();
753 }
754 ```
755 
756 ### Animation Targets
757 
758 ```
759 Transform/Opacity only ‚Üê What to animate
760 16.67ms per frame ‚Üê Time budget
761 60fps minimum ‚Üê Target
762 Low-end Android ‚Üê Test device
763 ```
764 
765 ---
766 
767 > **Remember:** Performance is not optimization‚Äîit's baseline quality. A slow app is a broken app. Test on the worst device your users have, not the best device you have.

=== FILE_CAPSULE_BEGIN FID:F108 path:skills/mobile-design/mobile-testing.md hash:a940bd0c2d5204f83b1b8e2214e938e2a4b0e68e72e7b63b175c33d7bb8bdd12 lines:356 ===
001 # Mobile Testing Patterns
002 
003 > **Mobile testing is NOT web testing. Different constraints, different strategies.**
004 > This file teaches WHEN to use each testing approach and WHY.
005 > **Code examples are minimal - focus on decision-making.**
006 
007 ---
008 
009 ## üß† MOBILE TESTING MINDSET
010 
011 ```
012 Mobile testing differs from web:
013 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Real devices matter (emulators hide bugs)
014 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Platform differences (iOS vs Android behavior)
015 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Network conditions vary wildly
016 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Battery/performance under test
017 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App lifecycle (background, killed, restored)
018 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Permissions and system dialogs
019 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Touch interactions vs clicks
020 ```
021 
022 ---
023 
024 ## üö´ AI MOBILE TESTING ANTI-PATTERNS
025 
026 | ‚ùå AI Default | Why It's Wrong | ‚úÖ Mobile-Correct |
027 |---------------|----------------|-------------------|
028 | Jest-only testing | Misses native layer | Jest + E2E on device |
029 | Enzyme patterns | Deprecated, web-focused | React Native Testing Library |
030 | Browser-based E2E (Cypress) | Can't test native features | Detox / Maestro |
031 | Mock everything | Misses integration bugs | Real device testing |
032 | Ignore platform tests | iOS/Android differ | Platform-specific cases |
033 | Skip performance tests | Mobile perf is critical | Profile on low-end device |
034 | Test only happy path | Mobile has more edge cases | Offline, permissions, interrupts |
035 | 100% unit test coverage | False security | Pyramid balance |
036 | Copy web testing patterns | Different environment | Mobile-specific tools |
037 
038 ---
039 
040 ## 1. Testing Tool Selection
041 
042 ### Decision Tree
043 
044 ```
045 WHAT ARE YOU TESTING?
046         ‚îÇ
047         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Pure functions, utilities, helpers
048         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Jest (unit tests)
049         ‚îÇ       ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ No special mobile setup needed
050         ‚îÇ
051         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Individual components (isolated)
052         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ React Native ‚Üí React Native Testing Library
053         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Flutter ‚Üí flutter_test (widget tests)
054         ‚îÇ
055         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Components with hooks, context, navigation
056         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ React Native ‚Üí RNTL + mocked providers
057         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Flutter ‚Üí integration_test package
058         ‚îÇ
059         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Full user flows (login, checkout, etc.)
060         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Detox (React Native, fast, reliable)
061         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Maestro (Cross-platform, YAML-based)
062         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Appium (Legacy, slow, last resort)
063         ‚îÇ
064         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance, memory, battery
065             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Flashlight (RN performance)
066             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Flutter DevTools
067             ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Real device profiling (Xcode/Android Studio)
068 ```
069 
070 ### Tool Comparison
071 
072 | Tool | Platform | Speed | Reliability | Use When |
073 |------|----------|-------|-------------|----------|
074 | **Jest** | RN | ‚ö°‚ö°‚ö° | ‚ö°‚ö°‚ö° | Unit tests, logic |
075 | **RNTL** | RN | ‚ö°‚ö°‚ö° | ‚ö°‚ö° | Component tests |
076 | **flutter_test** | Flutter | ‚ö°‚ö°‚ö° | ‚ö°‚ö°‚ö° | Widget tests |
077 | **Detox** | RN | ‚ö°‚ö° | ‚ö°‚ö°‚ö° | E2E, critical flows |
078 | **Maestro** | Both | ‚ö°‚ö° | ‚ö°‚ö° | E2E, cross-platform |
079 | **Appium** | Both | ‚ö° | ‚ö° | Legacy, last resort |
080 
081 ---
082 
083 ## 2. Testing Pyramid for Mobile
084 
085 ```
086                     ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
087                     ‚îÇ    E2E Tests  ‚îÇ  10%
088                     ‚îÇ  (Real device) ‚îÇ  Slow, expensive, essential
089                     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
090                     ‚îÇ  Integration  ‚îÇ  20%
091                     ‚îÇ    Tests      ‚îÇ  Component + context
092                     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
093                     ‚îÇ  Component    ‚îÇ  30%
094                     ‚îÇ    Tests      ‚îÇ  Isolated UI
095                     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
096                     ‚îÇ   Unit Tests  ‚îÇ  40%
097                     ‚îÇ    (Jest)     ‚îÇ  Pure logic
098                     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
099 ```
100 
101 ### Why This Distribution?
102 
103 | Level | Why This % |
104 |-------|------------|
105 | **E2E 10%** | Slow, flaky, but catches integration bugs |
106 | **Integration 20%** | Tests real user flows without full app |
107 | **Component 30%** | Fast feedback on UI changes |
108 | **Unit 40%** | Fastest, most stable, logic coverage |
109 
110 > üî¥ **If you have 90% unit tests and 0% E2E, you're testing the wrong things.**
111 
112 ---
113 
114 ## 3. What to Test at Each Level
115 
116 ### Unit Tests (Jest)
117 
118 ```
119 ‚úÖ TEST:
120 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Utility functions (formatDate, calculatePrice)
121 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ State reducers (Redux, Zustand stores)
122 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ API response transformers
123 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Validation logic
124 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Business rules
125 
126 ‚ùå DON'T TEST:
127 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Component rendering (use component tests)
128 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation (use integration tests)
129 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Native modules (mock them)
130 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Third-party libraries
131 ```
132 
133 ### Component Tests (RNTL / flutter_test)
134 
135 ```
136 ‚úÖ TEST:
137 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Component renders correctly
138 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User interactions (tap, type, swipe)
139 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Loading/error/empty states
140 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility labels exist
141 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Props change behavior
142 
143 ‚ùå DON'T TEST:
144 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Internal implementation details
145 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Snapshot everything (only key components)
146 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Styling specifics (brittle)
147 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Third-party component internals
148 ```
149 
150 ### Integration Tests
151 
152 ```
153 ‚úÖ TEST:
154 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Form submission flows
155 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation between screens
156 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ State persistence across screens
157 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ API integration (with mocked server)
158 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Context/provider interactions
159 
160 ‚ùå DON'T TEST:
161 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Every possible path (use unit tests)
162 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Third-party services (mock them)
163 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Backend logic (backend tests)
164 ```
165 
166 ### E2E Tests
167 
168 ```
169 ‚úÖ TEST:
170 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Critical user journeys (login, purchase, signup)
171 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Offline ‚Üí online transitions
172 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Deep link handling
173 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Push notification navigation
174 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Permission flows
175 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Payment flows
176 
177 ‚ùå DON'T TEST:
178 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Every edge case (too slow)
179 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Visual regression (use snapshot tests)
180 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Non-critical features
181 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Backend-only logic
182 ```
183 
184 ---
185 
186 ## 4. Platform-Specific Testing
187 
188 ### What Differs Between iOS and Android?
189 
190 | Area | iOS Behavior | Android Behavior | Test Both? |
191 |------|--------------|------------------|------------|
192 | **Back navigation** | Edge swipe | System back button | ‚úÖ YES |
193 | **Permissions** | Ask once, settings | Ask each time, rationale | ‚úÖ YES |
194 | **Keyboard** | Different appearance | Different behavior | ‚úÖ YES |
195 | **Date picker** | Wheel/modal | Material dialog | ‚ö†Ô∏è If custom UI |
196 | **Push format** | APNs payload | FCM payload | ‚úÖ YES |
197 | **Deep links** | Universal Links | App Links | ‚úÖ YES |
198 | **Gestures** | Some unique | Material gestures | ‚ö†Ô∏è If custom |
199 
200 ### Platform Testing Strategy
201 
202 ```
203 FOR EACH PLATFORM:
204 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Run unit tests (same on both)
205 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Run component tests (same on both)
206 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Run E2E on REAL DEVICE
207 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ iOS: iPhone (not just simulator)
208 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Android: Mid-range device (not flagship)
209 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Test platform-specific features separately
210 ```
211 
212 ---
213 
214 ## 5. Offline & Network Testing
215 
216 ### Offline Scenarios to Test
217 
218 | Scenario | What to Verify |
219 |----------|----------------|
220 | Start app offline | Shows cached data or offline message |
221 | Go offline mid-action | Action queued, not lost |
222 | Come back online | Queue synced, no duplicates |
223 | Slow network (2G) | Loading states, timeouts work |
224 | Flaky network | Retry logic, error recovery |
225 
226 ### How to Test Network Conditions
227 
228 ```
229 APPROACH:
230 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Unit tests: Mock NetInfo, test logic
231 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Integration: Mock API responses, test UI
232 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ E2E (Detox): Use device.setURLBlacklist()
233 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ E2E (Maestro): Use network conditions
234 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Manual: Use Charles Proxy / Network Link Conditioner
235 ```
236 
237 ---
238 
239 ## 6. Performance Testing
240 
241 ### What to Measure
242 
243 | Metric | Target | How to Measure |
244 |--------|--------|----------------|
245 | **App startup** | < 2 seconds | Profiler, Flashlight |
246 | **Screen transition** | < 300ms | React DevTools |
247 | **List scroll** | 60 FPS | Profiler, feel |
248 | **Memory** | Stable, no leaks | Instruments / Android Profiler |
249 | **Bundle size** | Minimize | Metro bundler analysis |
250 
251 ### When to Performance Test
252 
253 ```
254 PERFORMANCE TEST:
255 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Before release (required)
256 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ After adding heavy features
257 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ After upgrading dependencies
258 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ When users report slowness
259 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ On CI (optional, automated benchmarks)
260 
261 WHERE TO TEST:
262 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Real device (REQUIRED)
263 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Low-end device (Galaxy A series, old iPhone)
264 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ NOT on emulator (lies about performance)
265 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ With production-like data (not 3 items)
266 ```
267 
268 ---
269 
270 ## 7. Accessibility Testing
271 
272 ### What to Verify
273 
274 | Element | Check |
275 |---------|-------|
276 | Interactive elements | Have accessibilityLabel |
277 | Images | Have alt text or decorative flag |
278 | Forms | Labels linked to inputs |
279 | Buttons | Role = button |
280 | Touch targets | ‚â• 44x44 (iOS) / 48x48 (Android) |
281 | Color contrast | WCAG AA minimum |
282 
283 ### How to Test
284 
285 ```
286 AUTOMATED:
287 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ React Native: jest-axe
288 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Flutter: Accessibility checker in tests
289 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Lint rules for missing labels
290 
291 MANUAL:
292 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Enable VoiceOver (iOS) / TalkBack (Android)
293 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigate entire app with screen reader
294 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Test with increased text size
295 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Test with reduced motion
296 ```
297 
298 ---
299 
300 ## 8. CI/CD Integration
301 
302 ### What to Run Where
303 
304 | Stage | Tests | Devices |
305 |-------|-------|---------|
306 | **PR** | Unit + Component | None (fast) |
307 | **Merge to main** | + Integration | Simulator/Emulator |
308 | **Pre-release** | + E2E | Real devices (farm) |
309 | **Nightly** | Full suite | Device farm |
310 
311 ### Device Farm Options
312 
313 | Service | Pros | Cons |
314 |---------|------|------|
315 | **Firebase Test Lab** | Free tier, Google devices | Android focus |
316 | **AWS Device Farm** | Wide selection | Expensive |
317 | **BrowserStack** | Good UX | Expensive |
318 | **Local devices** | Free, reliable | Limited variety |
319 
320 ---
321 
322 ## üìù MOBILE TESTING CHECKLIST
323 
324 ### Before PR
325 - [ ] Unit tests for new logic
326 - [ ] Component tests for new UI
327 - [ ] No console.logs in tests
328 - [ ] Tests pass on CI
329 
330 ### Before Release
331 - [ ] E2E on real iOS device
332 - [ ] E2E on real Android device
333 - [ ] Tested on low-end device
334 - [ ] Offline scenarios verified
335 - [ ] Performance acceptable
336 - [ ] Accessibility verified
337 
338 ### What to Skip (Consciously)
339 - [ ] 100% coverage (aim for meaningful coverage)
340 - [ ] Every visual permutation (use snapshots sparingly)
341 - [ ] Third-party library internals
342 - [ ] Backend logic (separate tests)
343 
344 ---
345 
346 ## üéØ Testing Questions to Ask
347 
348 Before writing tests, answer:
349 
350 1. **What could break?** ‚Üí Test that
351 2. **What's critical for users?** ‚Üí E2E test that
352 3. **What's complex logic?** ‚Üí Unit test that
353 4. **What's platform-specific?** ‚Üí Test on both platforms
354 5. **What happens offline?** ‚Üí Test that scenario
355 
356 > **Remember:** Good mobile testing is about testing the RIGHT things, not EVERYTHING. A flaky E2E test is worse than no test. A failing unit test that catches a bug is worth 100 passing trivial tests.

=== FILE_CAPSULE_BEGIN FID:F109 path:skills/mobile-design/mobile-typography.md hash:40253bb17ed0bdacef06c0f0f27233ba03274aa1587f0c96215025aaefc0316a lines:433 ===
001 # Mobile Typography Reference
002 
003 > Type scale, system fonts, Dynamic Type, accessibility, and dark mode typography.
004 > **Typography failures are the #1 cause of unreadable mobile apps.**
005 
006 ---
007 
008 ## 1. Mobile Typography Fundamentals
009 
010 ### Why Mobile Type is Different
011 
012 ```
013 DESKTOP:                        MOBILE:
014 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 20-30" viewing distance     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 12-15" viewing distance
015 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large viewport              ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Small viewport, narrow
016 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Hover for details           ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tap/scroll for details
017 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Controlled lighting         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Variable (outdoor, etc.)
018 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Fixed font size             ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User-controlled sizing
019 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Long reading sessions       ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Quick scanning
020 ```
021 
022 ### Mobile Type Rules
023 
024 | Rule | Desktop | Mobile |
025 |------|---------|--------|
026 | **Minimum body size** | 14px | 16px (14pt/14sp) |
027 | **Maximum line length** | 75 characters | 40-60 characters |
028 | **Line height** | 1.4-1.5 | 1.4-1.6 (more generous) |
029 | **Font weight** | Varies | Regular dominant, bold sparingly |
030 | **Contrast** | AA (4.5:1) | AA minimum, AAA preferred |
031 
032 ---
033 
034 ## 2. System Fonts
035 
036 ### iOS: SF Pro Family
037 
038 ```
039 San Francisco (SF) Family:
040 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Pro Display: Large text (‚â• 20pt)
041 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Pro Text: Body text (< 20pt)
042 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Pro Rounded: Friendly contexts
043 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Mono: Monospace
044 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Compact: Apple Watch, compact UI
045 
046 Features:
047 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Optical sizing (auto-adjusts)
048 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dynamic tracking (spacing)
049 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tabular/proportional figures
050 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Excellent legibility
051 ```
052 
053 ### Android: Roboto Family
054 
055 ```
056 Roboto Family:
057 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto: Default sans-serif
058 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto Flex: Variable font
059 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto Serif: Serif option
060 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto Mono: Monospace
061 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto Condensed: Narrow spaces
062 
063 Features:
064 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Optimized for screens
065 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Wide language support
066 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Multiple weights
067 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Good at small sizes
068 ```
069 
070 ### When to Use System Fonts
071 
072 ```
073 ‚úÖ USE system fonts when:
074 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Brand doesn't mandate custom font
075 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reading efficiency is priority
076 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App feels native/integrated important
077 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Performance is critical
078 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Wide language support needed
079 
080 ‚ùå AVOID system fonts when:
081 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Brand identity requires custom
082 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Design differentiation needed
083 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Editorial/magazine style
084 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ (But still support accessibility)
085 ```
086 
087 ### Custom Font Considerations
088 
089 ```
090 If using custom fonts:
091 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Include all weights needed
092 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Subset for file size
093 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Test at all Dynamic Type sizes
094 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Provide fallback to system
095 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Test rendering quality
096 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Check language support
097 ```
098 
099 ---
100 
101 ## 3. Type Scale
102 
103 ### iOS Type Scale (Built-in)
104 
105 | Style | Size | Weight | Line Height |
106 |-------|------|--------|-------------|
107 | Large Title | 34pt | Bold | 41pt |
108 | Title 1 | 28pt | Bold | 34pt |
109 | Title 2 | 22pt | Bold | 28pt |
110 | Title 3 | 20pt | Semibold | 25pt |
111 | Headline | 17pt | Semibold | 22pt |
112 | Body | 17pt | Regular | 22pt |
113 | Callout | 16pt | Regular | 21pt |
114 | Subhead | 15pt | Regular | 20pt |
115 | Footnote | 13pt | Regular | 18pt |
116 | Caption 1 | 12pt | Regular | 16pt |
117 | Caption 2 | 11pt | Regular | 13pt |
118 
119 ### Android Type Scale (Material 3)
120 
121 | Role | Size | Weight | Line Height |
122 |------|------|--------|-------------|
123 | Display Large | 57sp | 400 | 64sp |
124 | Display Medium | 45sp | 400 | 52sp |
125 | Display Small | 36sp | 400 | 44sp |
126 | Headline Large | 32sp | 400 | 40sp |
127 | Headline Medium | 28sp | 400 | 36sp |
128 | Headline Small | 24sp | 400 | 32sp |
129 | Title Large | 22sp | 400 | 28sp |
130 | Title Medium | 16sp | 500 | 24sp |
131 | Title Small | 14sp | 500 | 20sp |
132 | Body Large | 16sp | 400 | 24sp |
133 | Body Medium | 14sp | 400 | 20sp |
134 | Body Small | 12sp | 400 | 16sp |
135 | Label Large | 14sp | 500 | 20sp |
136 | Label Medium | 12sp | 500 | 16sp |
137 | Label Small | 11sp | 500 | 16sp |
138 
139 ### Creating Custom Scale
140 
141 ```
142 If creating custom scale, use modular ratio:
143 
144 Recommended ratios:
145 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 1.125 (Major second): Dense UI
146 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 1.200 (Minor third): Compact
147 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 1.250 (Major third): Balanced (common)
148 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 1.333 (Perfect fourth): Spacious
149 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 1.500 (Perfect fifth): Dramatic
150 
151 Example with 1.25 ratio, 16px base:
152 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ xs: 10px (16 √∑ 1.25 √∑ 1.25)
153 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ sm: 13px (16 √∑ 1.25)
154 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ base: 16px
155 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ lg: 20px (16 √ó 1.25)
156 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ xl: 25px (16 √ó 1.25 √ó 1.25)
157 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 2xl: 31px
158 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 3xl: 39px
159 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ 4xl: 49px
160 ```
161 
162 ---
163 
164 ## 4. Dynamic Type / Text Scaling
165 
166 ### iOS Dynamic Type (MANDATORY)
167 
168 ```swift
169 // ‚ùå WRONG: Fixed size (doesn't scale)
170 Text("Hello")
171     .font(.system(size: 17))
172 
173 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: Dynamic Type
174 Text("Hello")
175     .font(.body) // Scales with user setting
176 
177 // Custom font with scaling
178 Text("Hello")
179     .font(.custom("MyFont", size: 17, relativeTo: .body))
180 ```
181 
182 ### Android Text Scaling (MANDATORY)
183 
184 ```
185 ALWAYS use sp for text:
186 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ sp = Scale-independent pixels
187 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Scales with user font preference
188 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ dp does NOT scale (don't use for text)
189 
190 User can scale from 85% to 200%:
191 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Default (100%): 14sp = 14dp
192 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Largest (200%): 14sp = 28dp
193 
194 Test at 200%!
195 ```
196 
197 ### Scaling Challenges
198 
199 ```
200 Problems at large text sizes:
201 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Text overflows containers
202 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Buttons become too tall
203 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons look small relative to text
204 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Layouts break
205 
206 Solutions:
207 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use flexible containers (not fixed height)
208 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Allow text wrapping
209 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Scale icons with text
210 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Test at extremes during development
211 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use scrollable containers for long text
212 ```
213 
214 ---
215 
216 ## 5. Typography Accessibility
217 
218 ### Minimum Sizes
219 
220 | Element | Minimum | Recommended |
221 |---------|---------|-------------|
222 | Body text | 14px/pt/sp | 16px/pt/sp |
223 | Secondary text | 12px/pt/sp | 13-14px/pt/sp |
224 | Captions | 11px/pt/sp | 12px/pt/sp |
225 | Buttons | 14px/pt/sp | 14-16px/pt/sp |
226 | **Nothing smaller** | 11px | - |
227 
228 ### Contrast Requirements (WCAG)
229 
230 ```
231 Normal text (< 18pt or < 14pt bold):
232 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ AA: 4.5:1 ratio minimum
233 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ AAA: 7:1 ratio recommended
234 
235 Large text (‚â• 18pt or ‚â• 14pt bold):
236 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ AA: 3:1 ratio minimum
237 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ AAA: 4.5:1 ratio recommended
238 
239 Logos/decorative: No requirement
240 ```
241 
242 ### Line Height for Accessibility
243 
244 ```
245 WCAG Success Criterion 1.4.12:
246 
247 Line height (line spacing): ‚â• 1.5√ó
248 Paragraph spacing: ‚â• 2√ó font size
249 Letter spacing: ‚â• 0.12√ó font size
250 Word spacing: ‚â• 0.16√ó font size
251 
252 Mobile recommendation:
253 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Body: 1.4-1.6 line height
254 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Headings: 1.2-1.3 line height
255 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Never below 1.2
256 ```
257 
258 ---
259 
260 ## 6. Dark Mode Typography
261 
262 ### Color Adjustments
263 
264 ```
265 Light Mode:               Dark Mode:
266 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Black text (#000)     ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ White/light gray (#E0E0E0)
267 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ High contrast         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Slightly reduced contrast
268 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Full saturation       ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Desaturated colors
269 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Dark = emphasis       ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Light = emphasis
270 
271 RULE: Don't use pure white (#FFF) on dark.
272 Use off-white (#E0E0E0 to #F0F0F0) to reduce eye strain.
273 ```
274 
275 ### Dark Mode Hierarchy
276 
277 | Level | Light Mode | Dark Mode |
278 |-------|------------|-----------|
279 | Primary text | #000000 | #E8E8E8 |
280 | Secondary text | #666666 | #A0A0A0 |
281 | Tertiary text | #999999 | #707070 |
282 | Disabled text | #CCCCCC | #505050 |
283 
284 ### Weight in Dark Mode
285 
286 ```
287 Dark mode text appears thinner due to halation
288 (light bleeding into dark background)
289 
290 Consider:
291 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Using medium weight for body (instead of regular)
292 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Increasing letter-spacing slightly
293 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Testing on actual OLED displays
294 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Using slightly bolder weight than light mode
295 ```
296 
297 ---
298 
299 ## 7. Typography Anti-Patterns
300 
301 ### ‚ùå Common Mistakes
302 
303 | Mistake | Problem | Fix |
304 |---------|---------|-----|
305 | **Fixed font sizes** | Ignores accessibility | Use dynamic sizing |
306 | **Too small text** | Unreadable | Min 14pt/sp |
307 | **Low contrast** | Invisible in sunlight | Min 4.5:1 |
308 | **Long lines** | Hard to track | Max 60 chars |
309 | **Tight line height** | Cramped, hard to read | Min 1.4√ó |
310 | **Too many sizes** | Visual chaos | Max 5-7 sizes |
311 | **All caps body** | Hard to read | Headlines only |
312 | **Light gray on white** | Impossible in bright light | Higher contrast |
313 
314 ### ‚ùå AI Typography Mistakes
315 
316 ```
317 AI tends to:
318 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use fixed px values instead of pt/sp
319 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Skip Dynamic Type support
320 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use too small text (12-14px body)
321 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Ignore line height settings
322 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use low contrast "aesthetic" grays
323 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Apply same scale to mobile as desktop
324 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Skip testing at large text sizes
325 
326 RULE: Typography must SCALE.
327 Test at smallest and largest settings.
328 ```
329 
330 ---
331 
332 ## 8. Font Loading & Performance
333 
334 ### Font File Optimization
335 
336 ```
337 Font file sizes matter on mobile:
338 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Full font: 100-300KB per weight
339 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Subset (Latin): 15-40KB per weight
340 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Variable font: 100-200KB (all weights)
341 
342 Recommendations:
343 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Subset to needed characters
344 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use WOFF2 format
345 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Max 2-3 font files
346 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Consider variable fonts
347 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Cache fonts appropriately
348 ```
349 
350 ### Loading Strategy
351 
352 ```
353 1. SYSTEM FONT FALLBACK
354    Show system font ‚Üí swap when custom loads
355 
356 2. FONT DISPLAY SWAP
357    font-display: swap (CSS)
358 
359 3. PRELOAD CRITICAL FONTS
360    Preload fonts needed above the fold
361 
362 4. DON'T BLOCK RENDER
363    Don't wait for fonts to show content
364 ```
365 
366 ---
367 
368 ## 9. Typography Checklist
369 
370 ### Before Any Text Design
371 
372 - [ ] Body text ‚â• 16px/pt/sp?
373 - [ ] Line height ‚â• 1.4?
374 - [ ] Line length ‚â§ 60 chars?
375 - [ ] Type scale defined (max 5-7 sizes)?
376 - [ ] Using pt (iOS) or sp (Android)?
377 
378 ### Before Release
379 
380 - [ ] Dynamic Type tested (iOS)?
381 - [ ] Font scaling tested at 200% (Android)?
382 - [ ] Dark mode contrast checked?
383 - [ ] Sunlight readability tested?
384 - [ ] All text has proper hierarchy?
385 - [ ] Custom fonts have fallbacks?
386 - [ ] Long text scrolls properly?
387 
388 ---
389 
390 ## 10. Quick Reference
391 
392 ### Typography Tokens
393 
394 ```
395 // iOS
396 .largeTitle  // 34pt, Bold
397 .title       // 28pt, Bold
398 .title2      // 22pt, Bold
399 .title3      // 20pt, Semibold
400 .headline    // 17pt, Semibold
401 .body        // 17pt, Regular
402 .subheadline // 15pt, Regular
403 .footnote    // 13pt, Regular
404 .caption     // 12pt, Regular
405 
406 // Android (Material 3)
407 displayLarge   // 57sp
408 headlineLarge  // 32sp
409 titleLarge     // 22sp
410 bodyLarge      // 16sp
411 labelLarge     // 14sp
412 ```
413 
414 ### Minimum Sizes
415 
416 ```
417 Body:       14-16pt/sp (16 preferred)
418 Secondary:  12-13pt/sp
419 Caption:    11-12pt/sp
420 Nothing:    < 11pt/sp
421 ```
422 
423 ### Line Height
424 
425 ```
426 Headings:  1.1-1.3
427 Body:      1.4-1.6
428 Long text: 1.5-1.75
429 ```
430 
431 ---
432 
433 > **Remember:** If users can't read your text, your app is broken. Typography isn't decoration‚Äîit's the primary interface. Test on real devices, in real conditions, with accessibility settings enabled.
