001 # Android Platform Guidelines
002 
003 > Material Design 3 essentials, Android design conventions, Roboto typography, and native patterns.
004 > **Read this file when building for Android devices.**
005 
006 ---
007 
008 ## 1. Material Design 3 Philosophy
009 
010 ### Core Material Principles
011 
012 ```
013 MATERIAL AS METAPHOR:
014 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Surfaces exist in 3D space
015 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Light and shadow define hierarchy
016 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Motion provides continuity
017 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Bold, graphic, intentional design
018 
019 ADAPTIVE DESIGN:
020 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Responds to device capabilities
021 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ One UI for all form factors
022 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dynamic color from wallpaper
023 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Personalized per user
024 
025 ACCESSIBLE BY DEFAULT:
026 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large touch targets
027 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Clear visual hierarchy
028 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Semantic colors
029 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Motion respects preferences
030 ```
031 
032 ### Material Design Values
033 
034 | Value | Implementation |
035 |-------|----------------|
036 | **Dynamic Color** | Colors adapt to wallpaper/user preference |
037 | **Personalization** | User-specific themes |
038 | **Accessibility** | Built into every component |
039 | **Responsiveness** | Works on all screen sizes |
040 | **Consistency** | Unified design language |
041 
042 ---
043 
044 ## 2. Android Typography
045 
046 ### Roboto Font Family
047 
048 ```
049 Android System Fonts:
050 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto: Default sans-serif
051 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto Flex: Variable font (API 33+)
052 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto Serif: Serif alternative
053 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Roboto Mono: Monospace
054 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Google Sans: Google products (special license)
055 ```
056 
057 ### Material Type Scale
058 
059 | Role | Size | Weight | Line Height | Usage |
060 |------|------|--------|-------------|-------|
061 | **Display Large** | 57sp | Regular | 64sp | Hero text, splash |
062 | **Display Medium** | 45sp | Regular | 52sp | Large headers |
063 | **Display Small** | 36sp | Regular | 44sp | Medium headers |
064 | **Headline Large** | 32sp | Regular | 40sp | Page titles |
065 | **Headline Medium** | 28sp | Regular | 36sp | Section headers |
066 | **Headline Small** | 24sp | Regular | 32sp | Subsections |
067 | **Title Large** | 22sp | Regular | 28sp | Dialogs, cards |
068 | **Title Medium** | 16sp | Medium | 24sp | Lists, navigation |
069 | **Title Small** | 14sp | Medium | 20sp | Tabs, secondary |
070 | **Body Large** | 16sp | Regular | 24sp | Primary content |
071 | **Body Medium** | 14sp | Regular | 20sp | Secondary content |
072 | **Body Small** | 12sp | Regular | 16sp | Captions |
073 | **Label Large** | 14sp | Medium | 20sp | Buttons, FAB |
074 | **Label Medium** | 12sp | Medium | 16sp | Navigation |
075 | **Label Small** | 11sp | Medium | 16sp | Chips, badges |
076 
077 ### Scalable Pixels (sp)
078 
079 ```
080 sp = Scale-independent pixels
081 
082 sp automatically scales with:
083 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User font size preference
084 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Display density
085 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility settings
086 
087 RULE: ALWAYS use sp for text, dp for everything else.
088 ```
089 
090 ### Font Weight Usage
091 
092 | Weight | Use Case |
093 |--------|----------|
094 | Regular (400) | Body text, display |
095 | Medium (500) | Buttons, labels, emphasis |
096 | Bold (700) | Rarely, strong emphasis only |
097 
098 ---
099 
100 ## 3. Material Color System
101 
102 ### Dynamic Color (Material You)
103 
104 ```
105 Android 12+ Dynamic Color:
106 
107 User's wallpaper ‚Üí Color extraction ‚Üí App theme
108 
109 Your app automatically adapts to:
110 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Primary color (from wallpaper)
111 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Secondary color (complementary)
112 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tertiary color (accent)
113 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Surface colors (derived)
114 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ All semantic colors adjust
115 
116 RULE: Implement dynamic color for personalized feel.
117 ```
118 
119 ### Semantic Color Roles
120 
121 ```
122 Surface Colors:
123 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Surface ‚Üí Main background
124 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SurfaceVariant ‚Üí Cards, containers
125 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SurfaceTint ‚Üí Elevation overlay
126 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ InverseSurface ‚Üí Snackbars, tooltips
127 
128 On-Surface Colors:
129 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ OnSurface ‚Üí Primary text
130 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ OnSurfaceVariant ‚Üí Secondary text
131 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Outline ‚Üí Borders, dividers
132 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ OutlineVariant ‚Üí Subtle dividers
133 
134 Primary Colors:
135 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Primary ‚Üí Key actions, FAB
136 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ OnPrimary ‚Üí Text on primary
137 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ PrimaryContainer ‚Üí Less emphasis
138 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ OnPrimaryContainer ‚Üí Text on container
139 
140 Secondary/Tertiary: Similar pattern
141 ```
142 
143 ### Error, Warning, Success Colors
144 
145 | Role | Light | Dark | Usage |
146 |------|-------|------|-------|
147 | Error | #B3261E | #F2B8B5 | Errors, destructive |
148 | OnError | #FFFFFF | #601410 | Text on error |
149 | ErrorContainer | #F9DEDC | #8C1D18 | Error backgrounds |
150 
151 ### Dark Theme
152 
153 ```
154 Material Dark Theme:
155 
156 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Background: #121212 (not pure black by default)
157 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Surface: #1E1E1E, #232323, etc. (elevation)
158 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Elevation: Higher = lighter overlay
159 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reduce saturation on colors
160 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Check contrast ratios
161 
162 Elevation overlays (dark mode):
163 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 0dp ‚Üí 0% overlay
164 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 1dp ‚Üí 5% overlay
165 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 3dp ‚Üí 8% overlay
166 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 6dp ‚Üí 11% overlay
167 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 8dp ‚Üí 12% overlay
168 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 12dp ‚Üí 14% overlay
169 ```
170 
171 ---
172 
173 ## 4. Android Layout & Spacing
174 
175 ### Layout Grid
176 
177 ```
178 Android uses 8dp baseline grid:
179 
180 All spacing in multiples of 8dp:
181 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 4dp: Component internal (half-step)
182 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 8dp: Minimum spacing
183 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 16dp: Standard spacing
184 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 24dp: Section spacing
185 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 32dp: Large spacing
186 
187 Margins:
188 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Compact (phone): 16dp
189 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Medium (small tablet): 24dp
190 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Expanded (large): 24dp+ or columns
191 ```
192 
193 ### Responsive Layout
194 
195 ```
196 Window Size Classes:
197 
198 COMPACT (< 600dp width):
199 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Phones in portrait
200 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Single column layout
201 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Bottom navigation
202 
203 MEDIUM (600-840dp width):
204 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tablets, foldables
205 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Consider 2 columns
206 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation rail option
207 
208 EXPANDED (> 840dp width):
209 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large tablets, desktop
210 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Multi-column layouts
211 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Navigation drawer
212 ```
213 
214 ### Canonical Layouts
215 
216 | Layout | Use Case | Window Class |
217 |--------|----------|--------------|
218 | **List-Detail** | Email, messages | Medium, Expanded |
219 | **Feed** | Social, news | All |
220 | **Supporting Pane** | Reference content | Medium, Expanded |
221

224 ## 5. Android Navigation Patterns
225 
226 ### Navigation Components
227 
228 | Component | Use Case | Position |
229 |-----------|----------|----------|
230 | **Bottom Navigation** | 3-5 top-level destinations | Bottom |
231 | **Navigation Rail** | Tablets, foldables | Left side, vertical |
232 | **Navigation Drawer** | Many destinations, large screens | Left side, hidden/visible |
233 | **Top App Bar** | Current context, actions | Top |
234 
235 ### Bottom Navigation
236 
237 ```
238 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
239 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
240 ‚îÇ         Content Area                ‚îÇ
241 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
242 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
243 ‚îÇ  üè†     üîç     ‚ûï     ‚ù§Ô∏è     üë§    ‚îÇ ‚Üê 80dp height
244 ‚îÇ Home   Search  FAB   Saved  Profile‚îÇ
245 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
246 
247 Rules:
248 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 3-5 destinations
249 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons: Material Symbols (24dp)
250 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Labels: Always visible (accessibility)
251 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Active: Filled icon + indicator pill
252 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Badge: For notifications
253 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ FAB can integrate (optional)
254 ```
255 
256 ### Top App Bar
257 
258 ```
259 Types:
260 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Center-aligned: Logo apps, simple
261 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Small: Compact, scrolls away
262 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Medium: Title + actions, collapses
263 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large: Display title, collapses to small
264 
265 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
266 ‚îÇ  ‚ò∞   App Title              üîî ‚ãÆ  ‚îÇ ‚Üê 64dp (small)
267 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
268 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
269 ‚îÇ         Content Area                ‚îÇ
270 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
271 
272 Actions: Max 3 icons, overflow menu ( ‚ãÆ ) for more
273 ```
274 
275 ### Navigation Rail (Tablets)
276 
277 ```
278 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¨‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
279 ‚îÇ  ‚â°    ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
280 ‚îÇ       ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
281 ‚îÇ  üè†   ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
282 ‚îÇ Home  ‚îÇ       Content Area          ‚îÇ
283 ‚îÇ       ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
284 ‚îÇ  üîç   ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
285 ‚îÇSearch ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
286 ‚îÇ       ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
287 ‚îÇ  üë§   ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
288 ‚îÇProfile‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ
289 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î¥‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
290 
291 Width: 80dp
292 Icons: 24dp
293 Labels: Below icon
294 FAB: Can be at top
295 ```
296 
297 ### Back Navigation
298 
299 ```
300 Android provides system back:
301 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Back button (3-button nav)
302 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Back gesture (swipe from edge)
303 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Predictive back (Android 14+)
304 
305 Your app must:
306 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Handle back correctly (pop stack)
307 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Support predictive back animation
308 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Never hijack/override back unexpectedly
309 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Confirm before discarding unsaved work
310 ```

314 ## 6. Material Components
315 
316 ### Buttons
317 
318 ```
319 Button Types:
320 
321 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
322 ‚îÇ    Filled Button     ‚îÇ  ‚Üê Primary action
323 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
324 
325 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
326 ‚îÇ    Tonal Button      ‚îÇ  ‚Üê Secondary, less emphasis
327 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
328 
329 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
330 ‚îÇ   Outlined Button    ‚îÇ  ‚Üê Tertiary, lower emphasis
331 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
332 
333     Text Button           ‚Üê Lowest emphasis
334 
335 Heights:
336 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Small: 40dp (when constrained)
337 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Standard: 40dp
338 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large: 56dp (FAB size when needed)
339 
340 Min touch target: 48dp (even if visual is smaller)
341 ```
342 
343 ### Floating Action Button (FAB)
344 
345 ```
346 FAB Types:
347 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Standard: 56dp diameter
348 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Small: 40dp diameter
349 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large: 96dp diameter
350 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Extended: Icon + text, variable width
351 
352 Position: Bottom right, 16dp from edges
353 Elevation: Floats above content
354 
355 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
356 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
357 ‚îÇ         Content                     ‚îÇ
358 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
359 ‚îÇ                              ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê ‚îÇ
360 ‚îÇ                              ‚îÇ ‚ûï ‚îÇ ‚îÇ ‚Üê FAB
361 ‚îÇ                              ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò ‚îÇ
362 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
363 ‚îÇ       Bottom Navigation             ‚îÇ
364 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
365 ```
366 
367 ### Cards
368 
369 ```
370 Card Types:
371 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Elevated: Shadow, resting state
372 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Filled: Background color, no shadow
373 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Outlined: Border, no shadow
374 
375 Card Anatomy:
376 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
377 ‚îÇ           Header Image              ‚îÇ ‚Üê Optional
378 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
379 ‚îÇ  Title / Headline                   ‚îÇ
380 ‚îÇ  Subhead / Supporting text          ‚îÇ
381 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
382 ‚îÇ      [ Action ]    [ Action ]       ‚îÇ ‚Üê Optional actions
383 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
384 
385 Corner radius: 12dp (M3 default)
386 Padding: 16dp
387 ```
388 
389 ### Text Fields
390 
391 ```
392 Types:
393 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Filled: Background fill, underline
394 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Outlined: Border all around
395 
396 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
397 ‚îÇ  Label                              ‚îÇ ‚Üê Floats up on focus
398 ‚îÇ  ________________________________________________
399 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ     Input text here...          ‚îÇ ‚Üê Leading/trailing icons
400 ‚îÇ  ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ‚Äæ
401 ‚îÇ  Supporting text or error           ‚îÇ
402 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
403 
404 Height: 56dp
405 Label: Animates from placeholder to top
406 Error: Red color + icon + message
407 ```
408 
409 ### Chips
410 
411 ```
412 Types:
413 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Assist: Smart actions (directions, call)
414 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Filter: Toggle filters
415 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Input: Represent entities (tags, contacts)
416 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Suggestion: Dynamic recommendations
417 
418 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
419 ‚îÇ  üè∑Ô∏è Filter   ‚îÇ  ‚Üê 32dp height, 8dp corner radius
420 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
421 
422 States: Unselected, Selected, Disabled
423 ```

427 ## 7. Android-Specific Patterns
428 
429 ### Snackbars
430 
431 ```
432 Position: Bottom, above navigation
433 Duration: 4-10 seconds
434 Action: One optional text action
435 
436 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
437 ‚îÇ  Archived 1 item                    [ UNDO ]    ‚îÇ
438 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
439 
440 Rules:
441 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Brief message, single line if possible
442 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Max 2 lines
443 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ One action (text, not icon)
444 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Can be dismissed by swipe
445 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Don't stack, queue them
446 ```
447 
448 ### Bottom Sheets
449 
450 ```
451 Types:
452 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Standard: Interactive content
453 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Modal: Blocks background (with scrim)
454 
455 Modal Bottom Sheet:
456 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
457 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
458 ‚îÇ        (Scrim over content)         ‚îÇ
459 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
460 ‚îú‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚ïê‚î§
461 ‚îÇ  ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ  (Drag handle, optional)     ‚îÇ
462 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
463 ‚îÇ        Sheet Content                ‚îÇ
464 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
465 ‚îÇ        Actions / Options            ‚îÇ
466 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
467 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
468 
469 Corner radius: 28dp (top corners)
470 ```
471 
472 ### Dialogs
473 
474 ```
475 Types:
476 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Basic: Title + content + actions
477 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Full-screen: Complex editing (mobile)
478 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Date/Time picker
479 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Confirmation dialog
480 
481 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
482 ‚îÇ              Title                  ‚îÇ
483 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
484 ‚îÇ       Supporting text that          ‚îÇ
485 ‚îÇ       explains the dialog           ‚îÇ
486 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
487 ‚îÇ           [ Cancel ]  [ Confirm ]   ‚îÇ
488 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
489 
490 Rules:
491 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Centered on screen
492 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Scrim behind (dim background)
493 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Max 2 actions aligned right
494 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Destructive action can be on left
495 ```
496 
497 ### Pull to Refresh
498 
499 ```
500 Android uses SwipeRefreshLayout pattern:
501 
502 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
503 ‚îÇ         ‚óã (Spinner)                 ‚îÇ ‚Üê Circular progress
504 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
505 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
506 ‚îÇ         Content                     ‚îÇ
507 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
508 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
509 
510 Spinner: Material circular indicator
511 Position: Top center, pulls down with content
512 ```
513 
514 ### Ripple Effect
515 
516 ```
517 Every touchable element needs ripple:
518 
519 Touch down ‚Üí Ripple expands from touch point
520 Touch up ‚Üí Ripple completes and fades
521 
522 Color:
523 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ On light: Black at ~12% opacity
524 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ On dark: White at ~12% opacity
525 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ On colored: Appropriate contrast
526 
527 This is MANDATORY for Android feel.
528 ```
529 
530 ---
531 
532 ## 8. Material Symbols
533 
534 ### Usage Guidelines
535 
536 ```
537 Material Symbols: Google's icon library
538 
539 Styles:
540 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Outlined: Default, most common
541 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Rounded: Softer, friendly
542 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Sharp: Angular, precise
543 
544 Variable font axes:
545 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ FILL: 0 (outline) to 1 (filled)
546 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ wght: 100-700 (weight)
547 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ GRAD: -25 to 200 (emphasis)
548 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ opsz: 20, 24, 40, 48 (optical size)
549 ```
550 
551 ### Icon Sizes
552 
553 | Size | Usage |
554 |------|-------|
555 | 20dp | Dense UI, inline |
556 | 24dp | Standard (most common) |
557 | 40dp | Larger touch targets |
558 | 48dp | Emphasis, standalone |
559 
560 ### States
561 
562 ```
563 Icon States:
564 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Default: Full opacity
565 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Disabled: 38% opacity
566 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Hover/Focus: Container highlight
567 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Selected: Filled variant + tint
568 
569 Active vs Inactive:
570 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Inactive: Outlined
571 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Active: Filled + indicator
572 ```
573 
574 ---
575 
576 ## 9. Android Accessibility
577 
578 ### TalkBack Requirements
579 
580 ```
581 Every interactive element needs:
582 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ contentDescription (what it is)
583 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Correct semantics (button, checkbox, etc.)
584 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ State announcements (selected, disabled)
585 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Grouping where logical
586 
587 Jetpack Compose:
588 Modifier.semantics {
589     contentDescription = "Play button"
590     role = Role.Button
591 }
592 
593 React Native:
594 accessibilityLabel="Play button"
595 accessibilityRole="button"
596 accessibilityState={{ disabled: false }}
597 ```
598 
599 ### Touch Target Size
600 
601 ```
602 MANDATORY: 48dp √ó 48dp minimum
603 
604 Even if visual element is smaller:
605 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icon: 24dp visual, 48dp touch area
606 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Checkbox: 20dp visual, 48dp touch area
607 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Add padding to reach 48dp
608 
609 Spacing between targets: 8dp minimum
610 ```
611 
612 ### Font Scaling
613 
614 ```
615 Android supports font scaling:
616 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 85% (smaller)
617 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 100% (default)
618 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 115%, 130%, 145%...
619 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Up to 200% (largest)
620 
621 RULE: Test your UI at 200% font scale.
622 Use sp units and avoid fixed heights.
623 ```
624 
625 ### Reduce Motion
626 
627 ```kotlin
628 // Check motion preference
629 val reduceMotion = Settings.Global.getFloat(
630     contentResolver,
631     Settings.Global.ANIMATOR_DURATION_SCALE,
632     1f
633 ) == 0f
634 
635 if (reduceMotion) {
636     // Skip or reduce animations
637 }
638 ```
639

641 
642 ## 10. Android Checklist
643 
644 ### Before Every Android Screen
645 
646 - [ ] Using Material 3 components
647 - [ ] Touch targets ‚â• 48dp
648 - [ ] Ripple effect on all touchables
649 - [ ] Roboto or Material type scale
650 - [ ] Semantic colors (dynamic color support)
651 - [ ] Back navigation works correctly
652 
653 ### Before Android Release
654 
655 - [ ] Dark theme tested
656 - [ ] Dynamic color tested (if supported)
657 - [ ] All font sizes tested (200% scale)
658 - [ ] TalkBack tested
659 - [ ] Predictive back implemented (Android 14+)
660 - [ ] Edge-to-edge display (Android 15+)
661 - [ ] Different screen sizes tested (phones, tablets)
662 - [ ] Navigation patterns match platform (back, gestures)
663 
664 ---
665 
666 > **Remember:** Android users expect Material Design. Custom designs that ignore Material patterns feel foreign and broken. Use Material components as your foundation, customize thoughtfully.

=== FILE_CAPSULE_BEGIN FID:F111 path:skills/mobile-design/platform-ios.md hash:3843ee18984f68ab5fa022976f2015429788baff5f8af0dd56d6298792e09396 lines:561 ===
001 # iOS Platform Guidelines
002 
003 > Human Interface Guidelines (HIG) essentials, iOS design conventions, SF Pro typography, and native patterns.
004 > **Read this file when building for iPhone/iPad.**
005 
006 ---
007 
008 ## 1. Human Interface Guidelines Philosophy
009 
010 ### Core Apple Design Principles
011 
012 ```
013 CLARITY:
014 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Text is legible at every size
015 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons are precise and lucid
016 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Adornments are subtle and appropriate
017 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Focus on functionality drives design
018 
019 DEFERENCE:
020 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ UI helps people understand and interact
021 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Content fills the screen
022 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ UI never competes with content
023 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Translucency hints at more content
024 
025 DEPTH:
026 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Distinct visual layers convey hierarchy
027 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Transitions provide sense of depth
028 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Touch reveals functionality
029 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Content is elevated over UI
030 ```
031 
032 ### iOS Design Values
033 
034 | Value | Implementation |
035 |-------|----------------|
036 | **Aesthetic Integrity** | Design matches function (game ‚â† productivity) |
037 | **Consistency** | Use system controls, familiar patterns |
038 | **Direct Manipulation** | Touch directly affects content |
039 | **Feedback** | Actions are acknowledged |
040 | **Metaphors** | Real-world comparisons aid understanding |
041 | **User Control** | User initiates actions, can cancel |
042 
043 ---
044 
045 ## 2. iOS Typography
046 
047 ### SF Pro Font Family
048 
049 ```
050 iOS System Fonts:
051 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Pro Text: Body text (< 20pt)
052 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Pro Display: Large titles (‚â• 20pt)
053 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Pro Rounded: Friendly contexts
054 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Mono: Code, tabular data
055 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ SF Compact: Apple Watch, smaller screens
056 ```
057 
058 ### iOS Type Scale (Dynamic Type)
059 
060 | Style | Default Size | Weight | Usage |
061 |-------|--------------|--------|-------|
062 | **Large Title** | 34pt | Bold | Navigation bar (scroll collapse) |
063 | **Title 1** | 28pt | Bold | Page titles |
064 | **Title 2** | 22pt | Bold | Section headers |
065 | **Title 3** | 20pt | Semibold | Subsection headers |
066 | **Headline** | 17pt | Semibold | Emphasized body |
067 | **Body** | 17pt | Regular | Primary content |
068 | **Callout** | 16pt | Regular | Secondary content |
069 | **Subhead** | 15pt | Regular | Tertiary content |
070 | **Footnote** | 13pt | Regular | Caption, timestamps |
071 | **Caption 1** | 12pt | Regular | Annotations |
072 | **Caption 2** | 11pt | Regular | Fine print |
073 
074 ### Dynamic Type Support (MANDATORY)
075 
076 ```swift
077 // ‚ùå WRONG: Fixed font size
078 Text("Hello")
079     .font(.system(size: 17))
080 
081 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: Dynamic Type
082 Text("Hello")
083     .font(.body) // Scales with user settings
084 
085 // React Native equivalent
086 <Text style={{ fontSize: 17 }}> // ‚ùå Fixed
087 <Text style={styles.body}> // Use a dynamic scale system
088 ```
089 
090 ### Font Weight Usage
091 
092 | Weight | iOS Constant | Use Case |
093 |--------|--------------|----------|
094 | Regular (400) | `.regular` | Body text |
095 | Medium (500) | `.medium` | Buttons, emphasis |
096 | Semibold (600) | `.semibold` | Subheadings |
097 | Bold (700) | `.bold` | Titles, key info |
098 | Heavy (800) | `.heavy` | Rarely, marketing |
099 
100 ---
101 
102 ## 3. iOS Color System
103 
104 ### System Colors (Semantic)
105 
106 ```
107 Use semantic colors for automatic dark mode:
108 
109 Primary:
110 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .label ‚Üí Primary text
111 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .secondaryLabel ‚Üí Secondary text
112 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .tertiaryLabel ‚Üí Tertiary text
113 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .quaternaryLabel ‚Üí Watermarks
114 
115 Backgrounds:
116 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .systemBackground ‚Üí Main background
117 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .secondarySystemBackground ‚Üí Grouped content
118 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .tertiarySystemBackground ‚Üí Elevated content
119 
120 Fills:
121 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .systemFill ‚Üí Large shapes
122 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .secondarySystemFill ‚Üí Medium shapes
123 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .tertiarySystemFill ‚Üí Small shapes
124 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .quaternarySystemFill ‚Üí Subtle shapes
125 ```
126 
127 ### System Accent Colors
128 
129 | Color | Light Mode | Dark Mode | Usage |
130 |-------|------------|-----------|-------|
131 | Blue | #007AFF | #0A84FF | Links, highlights, default tint |
132 | Green | #34C759 | #30D158 | Success, positive |
133 | Red | #FF3B30 | #FF453A | Errors, destructive |
134 | Orange | #FF9500 | #FF9F0A | Warnings |
135 | Yellow | #FFCC00 | #FFD60A | Attention |
136 | Purple | #AF52DE | #BF5AF2 | Special features |
137 | Pink | #FF2D55 | #FF375F | Affection, favorites |
138 | Teal | #5AC8FA | #64D2FF | Information |
139 
140 ### Dark Mode Considerations
141 
142 ```
143 iOS Dark Mode is not inverted light mode:
144 
145 LIGHT MODE:              DARK MODE:
146 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ White backgrounds    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ True black (#000) or near-black
147 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ High saturation      ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Desaturated colors
148 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Black text           ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ White/light gray text
149 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Drop shadows         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Glows or no shadows
150 
151 RULE: Always use semantic colors for automatic adaptation.
152 ```
153

155 
156 ## 4. iOS Layout & Spacing
157 
158 ### Safe Areas
159 
160 ```
161 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê

175 
176 ### Standard Margins & Padding
177 
178 | Element | Margin | Notes |
179 |---------|--------|-------|
180 | Screen edge ‚Üí content | 16pt | Standard horizontal margin |
181 | Grouped table sections | 16pt top/bottom | Breathing room |
182 | List item padding | 16pt horizontal | Standard cell padding |
183 | Card internal padding | 16pt | Content within cards |
184 | Button internal padding | 12pt vertical, 16pt horizontal | Minimum |
185 
186 ### iOS Grid System
187 
188 ```
189 iPhone Grid (Standard):
190 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 16pt margins (left/right)
191 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 8pt minimum spacing
192 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Content in 8pt multiples
193 
194 iPhone Grid (Compact):
195 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 8pt margins (when needed)
196 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 4pt minimum spacing
197 
198 iPad Grid:
199 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 20pt margins (or more)
200 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Consider multi-column layouts
201 ```

204 
205 ## 5. iOS Navigation Patterns
206 
207 ### Navigation Types
208 
209 | Pattern | Use Case | Implementation |
210 |---------|----------|----------------|
211 | **Tab Bar** | 3-5 top-level sections | Bottom, always visible |
212 | **Navigation Controller** | Hierarchical drill-down | Stack-based, back button |
213 | **Modal** | Focused task, interruption | Sheet or full-screen |
214 | **Sidebar** | iPad, multi-column | Left sidebar (iPad) |
215 
216 ### Tab Bar Guidelines
217 
218 ```
219 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
220 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
221 ‚îÇ         Content Area                ‚îÇ
222 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
223 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
224 ‚îÇ  üè†     üîç     ‚ûï     ‚ù§Ô∏è     üë§    ‚îÇ ‚Üê Tab bar (49pt height)
225 ‚îÇ Home   Search  New   Saved  Profile ‚îÇ
226 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
227 
228 Rules:
229 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ 3-5 items maximum
230 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Icons: SF Symbols or custom (25√ó25pt)
231 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Labels: Always include (accessibility)
232 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Active state: Filled icon + tint color
233 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Tab bar always visible (don't hide on scroll)
234 ```
235 
236 ### Navigation Bar Guidelines
237 
238 ```
239 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
240 ‚îÇ < Back     Page Title      Edit    ‚îÇ ‚Üê Navigation bar (44pt)
241 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
242 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
243 ‚îÇ         Content Area                ‚îÇ
244 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
245 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
246 
247 Rules:
248 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Back button: System chevron + previous title (or "Back")
249 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Title: Centered, dynamic font
250 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Right actions: Max 2 items
251 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large title: Collapses on scroll (optional)
252 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Prefer text buttons over icons (clarity)
253 ```
254 
255 ### Modal Presentations
256 
257 | Style | Use Case | Appearance |
258 |-------|----------|------------|
259 | **Sheet (default)** | Secondary tasks | Card slides up, parent visible |
260 | **Full Screen** | Immersive tasks | Covers entire screen |
261 | **Popover** | iPad, quick info | Arrow-pointed bubble |
262 | **Alert** | Critical interruption | Centered dialog |
263 | **Action Sheet** | Choices from context | Bottom sheet with options |
264 
265 ### Gestures
266 
267 | Gesture | iOS Convention |
268 |---------|----------------|
269 | **Edge swipe (left)** | Navigate back |
270 | **Pull down (sheet)** | Dismiss modal |
271 | **Long press** | Context menu |
272 | **Deep press** | Peek/Pop (legacy) |
273 | **Two-finger swipe** | Scroll in nested scroll |

355 ## 7. iOS Specific Patterns
356 
357 ### Pull to Refresh
358 
359 ```
360 Native UIRefreshControl behavior:
361 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Pull beyond threshold ‚Üí Spinner appears
362 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Release ‚Üí Refresh action triggered
363 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Loading state ‚Üí Spinner spins
364 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Complete ‚Üí Spinner disappears
365 
366 RULE: Always use native UIRefreshControl (don't custom build).
367 ```
368 
369 ### Swipe Actions
370 
371 ```
372 iOS swipe actions:
373 
374 ‚Üê Swipe Left (Destructive)      Swipe Right (Constructive) ‚Üí
375 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
376 ‚îÇ                    List Item Content                        ‚îÇ
377 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
378 
379 Left swipe reveals: Archive, Delete, Flag
380 Right swipe reveals: Pin, Star, Mark as Read
381 
382 Full swipe: Triggers first action
383 ```
384

432 ## 8. SF Symbols
433 
434 ### Usage Guidelines
435 
436 ```
437 SF Symbols: Apple's icon library (5000+ icons)
438 
439 Weights: Match text weight
440 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Ultralight / Thin / Light
441 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Regular / Medium / Semibold
442 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Bold / Heavy / Black
443 
444 Scales:
445 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .small ‚Üí Inline with small text
446 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .medium ‚Üí Standard UI
447 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .large ‚Üí Emphasis, standalone
448 ```
449 
450 ### Symbol Configurations
451 
452 ```swift
453 // SwiftUI
454 Image(systemName: "star.fill")
455     .font(.title2)
456     .foregroundStyle(.yellow)
457 
458 // With rendering mode
459 Image(systemName: "heart.fill")
460     .symbolRenderingMode(.multicolor)
461 
462 // Animated (iOS 17+)
463 Image(systemName: "checkmark.circle")
464     .symbolEffect(.bounce)
465 ```
466 
467 ### Symbol Best Practices
468 
469 | Guideline | Implementation |
470 |-----------|----------------|
471 | Match text weight | Symbol weight = font weight |
472 | Use standard symbols | Users recognize them |
473 | Multicolor when meaningful | Not just decoration |
474 | Fallback for older iOS | Check availability |
475 
476 ---
477 
478 ## 9. iOS Accessibility
479 
480 ### VoiceOver Requirements
481 
482 ```
483 Every interactive element needs:
484 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility label (what it is)
485 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility hint (what it does) - optional
486 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility traits (button, link, etc.)
487 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility value (current state)
488 
489 SwiftUI:
490 .accessibilityLabel("Play")
491 .accessibilityHint("Plays the selected track")
492 
493 React Native:
494 accessibilityLabel="Play"
495 accessibilityHint="Plays the selected track"
496 accessibilityRole="button"
497 ```
498 
499 ### Dynamic Type Scaling
500 
501 ```
502 MANDATORY: Support Dynamic Type
503 
504 Users can set text size from:
505 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ xSmall ‚Üí 14pt body
506 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Small ‚Üí 15pt body
507 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Medium ‚Üí 16pt body
508 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Large (Default) ‚Üí 17pt body
509 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ xLarge ‚Üí 19pt body
510 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ xxLarge ‚Üí 21pt body
511 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ xxxLarge ‚Üí 23pt body
512 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility sizes ‚Üí up to 53pt
513 
514 Your app MUST scale gracefully at all sizes.
515 ```
516 
517 ### Reduce Motion
518 
519 ```
520 Respect motion preferences:
521 
522 @Environment(\.accessibilityReduceMotion) var reduceMotion
523 
524 if reduceMotion {
525     // Use instant transitions
526 } else {
527     // Use animations
528 }
529 
530 React Native:
531 import { AccessibilityInfo } from 'react-native';
532 AccessibilityInfo.isReduceMotionEnabled()
533 ```
534 
535 ---
536 
537 ## 10. iOS Checklist
538 
539 ### Before Every iOS Screen
540 
541 - [ ] Using SF Pro or SF Symbols
542 - [ ] Dynamic Type supported
543 - [ ] Safe areas respected
544 - [ ] Navigation follows HIG (back gesture works)
545 - [ ] Tab bar items ‚â§ 5
546 - [ ] Touch targets ‚â• 44pt
547 
548 ### Before iOS Release
549 
550 - [ ] Dark mode tested
551 - [ ] All text sizes tested (Accessibility Inspector)
552 - [ ] VoiceOver tested
553 - [ ] Edge swipe back works everywhere
554 - [ ] Keyboard avoidance implemented
555 - [ ] Notch/Dynamic Island handled
556 - [ ] Home indicator area respected
557 - [ ] Native components used where possible
558 
559 ---
560 
561 > **Remember:** iOS users have strong expectations from other iOS apps. Deviating from HIG patterns feels "broken" to them. When in doubt, use the native component.

008 
009 > **Philosophy:** Touch-first. Battery-conscious. Platform-respectful. Offline-capable.

059 ## ‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL: ASK BEFORE ASSUMING (MANDATORY)
060 
061 > **STOP! If the user's request is open-ended, DO NOT default to your favorites.**
062 
063 ### You MUST Ask If Not Specified:
064 
065 | Aspect | Ask | Why |
066 |--------|-----|-----|
067 | **Platform** | "iOS, Android, or both?" | Affects EVERY design decision |
068 | **Framework** | "React Native, Flutter, or native?" | Determines patterns and tools |
069 | **Navigation** | "Tab bar, drawer, or stack-based?" | Core UX decision |
070 | **State** | "What state management? (Zustand/Redux/Riverpod/BLoC?)" | Architecture foundation |
071 | **Offline** | "Does this need to work offline?" | Affects data strategy |
072 | **Target devices** | "Phone only, or tablet support?" | Layout complexity |
073 
074 ### ‚õî AI MOBILE ANTI-PATTERNS (YASAK Lƒ∞STESƒ∞)
075 
076 > üö´ **These are AI default tendencies that MUST be avoided!**
077 
078 #### Performance Sins
079 
080 | ‚ùå NEVER DO | Why It's Wrong | ‚úÖ ALWAYS DO |
081 |-------------|----------------|--------------|
082 | **ScrollView for long lists** | Renders ALL items, memory explodes | Use `FlatList` / `FlashList` / `ListView.builder` |
083 | **Inline renderItem function** | New function every render, all items re-render | `useCallback` + `React.memo` |
084 | **Missing keyExtractor** | Index-based keys cause bugs on reorder | Unique, stable ID from data |
085 | **Skip getItemLayout** | Async layout = janky scroll | Provide when items have fixed height |
086 | **setState() everywhere** | Unnecessary widget rebuilds | Targeted state, `const` constructors |
087 | **Native driver: false** | Animations blocked by JS thread | `useNativeDriver: true` always |
088 | **console.log in production** | Blocks JS thread severely | Remove before release build |
089 | **Skip React.memo/const** | Every item re-renders on any change | Memoize list items ALWAYS |
090 
091 #### Touch/UX Sins
092 
093 | ‚ùå NEVER DO | Why It's Wrong | ‚úÖ ALWAYS DO |
094 |-------------|----------------|--------------|
095 | **Touch target < 44px** | Impossible to tap accurately, frustrating | Minimum 44pt (iOS) / 48dp (Android) |
096 | **Spacing < 8px between targets** | Accidental taps on neighbors | Minimum 8-12px gap |
097 | **Gesture-only interactions** | Motor impaired users excluded | Always provide button alternative |
098 | **No loading state** | User thinks app crashed | ALWAYS show loading feedback |
099 | **No error state** | User stuck, no recovery path | Show error with retry option |
100 | **No offline handling** | Crash/block when network lost | Graceful degradation, cached data |
101 | **Ignore platform conventions** | Users confused, muscle memory broken | iOS feels iOS, Android feels Android |
102 
103 #### Security Sins
104 
105 | ‚ùå NEVER DO | Why It's Wrong | ‚úÖ ALWAYS DO |
106 |-------------|----------------|--------------|
107 | **Token in AsyncStorage** | Easily accessible, stolen on rooted device | `SecureStore` / `Keychain` / `EncryptedSharedPreferences` |
108 | **Hardcode API keys** | Reverse engineered from APK/IPA | Environment variables, secure storage |
109 | **Skip SSL pinning** | MITM attacks possible | Pin certificates in production |
110 | **Log sensitive data** | Logs can be extracted | Never log tokens, passwords, PII |
111 
112 #### Architecture Sins
113 
114 | ‚ùå NEVER DO | Why It's Wrong | ‚úÖ ALWAYS DO |
115 |-------------|----------------|--------------|
116 | **Business logic in UI** | Untestable, unmaintainable | Service layer separation |
117 | **Global state for everything** | Unnecessary re-renders, complexity | Local state default, lift when needed |
118 | **Deep linking as afterthought** | Notifications, shares broken | Plan deep links from day one |
119 | **Skip dispose/cleanup** | Memory leaks, zombie listeners | Clean up subscriptions, timers |
120 
121 ---

123 ## üì± Platform Decision Matrix
124 
125 ### When to Unify vs Diverge
126 
127 ```
128                     UNIFY (same on both)          DIVERGE (platform-specific)
129                     ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ           ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
130 Business Logic      ‚úÖ Always                     -
131 Data Layer          ‚úÖ Always                     -
132 Core Features       ‚úÖ Always                     -
133 
134 Navigation          -                             ‚úÖ iOS: edge swipe, Android: back button
135 Gestures            -                             ‚úÖ Platform-native feel
136 Icons               -                             ‚úÖ SF Symbols vs Material Icons
137 Date Pickers        -                             ‚úÖ Native pickers feel right
138 Modals/Sheets       -                             ‚úÖ iOS: bottom sheet vs Android: dialog
139 Typography          -                             ‚úÖ SF Pro vs Roboto (or custom)
140 Error Dialogs       -                             ‚úÖ Platform conventions for alerts
141 ```
142 
143 ### Quick Reference: Platform Defaults
144 
145 | Element | iOS | Android |
146 |---------|-----|---------|
147 | **Primary Font** | SF Pro / SF Compact | Roboto |
148 | **Min Touch Target** | 44pt √ó 44pt | 48dp √ó 48dp |
149 | **Back Navigation** | Edge swipe left | System back button/gesture |
150 | **Bottom Tab Icons** | SF Symbols | Material Symbols |
151 | **Action Sheet** | UIActionSheet from bottom | Bottom Sheet / Dialog |
152 | **Progress** | Spinner | Linear progress (Material) |
153 | **Pull to Refresh** | Native UIRefreshControl | SwipeRefreshLayout |

156 
157 ## üß† Mobile UX Psychology (Quick Reference)
158 
159 ### Fitts' Law for Touch
160 
161 ```
162 Desktop: Cursor is precise (1px)
163 Mobile:  Finger is imprecise (~7mm contact area)
164 
165 ‚Üí Touch targets MUST be 44-48px minimum
166 ‚Üí Important actions in THUMB ZONE (bottom of screen)
167 ‚Üí Destructive actions AWAY from easy reach
168 ```
169 
170 ### Thumb Zone (One-Handed Usage)
171 
172 ```
173 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
174 ‚îÇ      HARD TO REACH          ‚îÇ ‚Üê Navigation, menu, back
175 ‚îÇ        (stretch)            ‚îÇ
176 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
177 ‚îÇ      OK TO REACH            ‚îÇ ‚Üê Secondary actions
178 ‚îÇ       (natural)             ‚îÇ
179 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§
180 ‚îÇ      EASY TO REACH          ‚îÇ ‚Üê PRIMARY CTAs, tab bar
181 ‚îÇ    (thumb's natural arc)    ‚îÇ ‚Üê Main content interaction
182 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
183         [  HOME  ]
184 ```
185 
186 ### Mobile-Specific Cognitive Load
187 
188 | Desktop | Mobile Difference |
189 |---------|-------------------|
190 | Multiple windows | ONE task at a time |
191 | Keyboard shortcuts | Touch gestures |
192 | Hover states | NO hover (tap or nothing) |
193 | Large viewport | Limited space, scroll vertical |
194 | Stable attention | Interrupted constantly |
195 
196 For deep dive: [touch-psychology.md](touch-psychology.md)
197

199 
200 ## ‚ö° Performance Principles (Quick Reference)
201 
202 ### React Native Critical Rules
203 
204 ```typescript
205 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: Memoized renderItem + React.memo wrapper
206 const ListItem = React.memo(({ item }: { item: Item }) => (
207   <View style={styles.item}>
208     <Text>{item.title}</Text>
209   </View>
210 ));
211 
212 const renderItem = useCallback(
213   ({ item }: { item: Item }) => <ListItem item={item} />,
214   []
215 );
216 
217 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: FlatList with all optimizations
218 <FlatList
219   data={items}
220   renderItem={renderItem}
221   keyExtractor={(item) => item.id}  // Stable ID, NOT index
222   getItemLayout={(data, index) => ({
223     length: ITEM_HEIGHT,
224     offset: ITEM_HEIGHT * index,
225     index,
226   })}
227   removeClippedSubviews={true}
228   maxToRenderPerBatch={10}
229   windowSize={5}
230 />
231 ```
232 
233 ### Flutter Critical Rules
234 
235 ```dart
236 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: const constructors prevent rebuilds
237 class MyWidget extends StatelessWidget {
238   const MyWidget({super.key}); // CONST!
239 
240   @override
241   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
242     return const Column( // CONST!
243       children: [
244         Text('Static content'),
245         MyConstantWidget(),
246       ],
247     );
248   }
249 }
250 
251 // ‚úÖ CORRECT: Targeted state with ValueListenableBuilder
252 ValueListenableBuilder<int>(
253   valueListenable: counter,
254   builder: (context, value, child) => Text('$value'),
255   child: const ExpensiveWidget(), // Won't rebuild!
256 )
257 ```
258 
259 ### Animation Performance
260 
261 ```
262 GPU-accelerated (FAST):     CPU-bound (SLOW):
263 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ transform               ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ width, height
264 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ opacity                 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ top, left, right, bottom
265 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ (use these ONLY)        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ margin, padding
266                             ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ (AVOID animating these)
267 ```
268 
269 For complete guide: [mobile-performance.md](mobile-performance.md)
270

278 üß† CHECKPOINT:

283

286 2. _______________
287 3. _______________

290 1. _______________
291 2. _______________
292 ```
293 
294 **Example:**
295 ```
296 üß† CHECKPOINT:
297 
298 Platform:   iOS + Android (Cross-platform)
299 Framework:  React Native + Expo
300 Files Read: touch-psychology.md, mobile-performance.md, platform-ios.md, platform-android.md
301 
302 3 Principles I Will Apply:
303 1. FlatList with React.memo + useCallback for all lists
304 2. 48px touch targets, thumb zone for primary CTAs
305 3. Platform-specific navigation (edge swipe iOS, back button Android)
306 
307 Anti-Patterns I Will Avoid:
308 1. ScrollView for lists ‚Üí FlatList
309 2. Inline renderItem ‚Üí Memoized
310 3. AsyncStorage for tokens ‚Üí SecureStore
311 ```

319 ```
320 WHAT ARE YOU BUILDING?
321         ‚îÇ
322         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Need OTA updates + rapid iteration + web team
323         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ React Native + Expo
324         ‚îÇ

326         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ Flutter
327         ‚îÇ

329         ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ iOS only ‚Üí SwiftUI
330         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Android only ‚Üí Kotlin + Jetpack Compose
331         ‚îÇ
332         ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Existing RN codebase + new features
333         ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ React Native (bare workflow)
334         ‚îÇ
335         ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Enterprise + existing Flutter codebase
336             ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ‚úÖ Flutter
337 ```

360 - [ ] **Error state with retry exists?**
361 - [ ] **Offline handling considered?**
362 - [ ] **Platform conventions followed?**

364 ### Before Release
365 
366 - [ ] **console.log removed?**
367 - [ ] **SecureStore for sensitive data?**
368 - [ ] **SSL pinning enabled?**
369 - [ ] **Lists optimized (memo, keyExtractor)?**
370 - [ ] **Memory cleanup on unmount?**

=== FILE_CAPSULE_BEGIN FID:F113 path:skills/mobile-design/touch-psychology.md hash:ec131aea1ce39b8d46d1c491ee4839510979d2f60ee7698e2ad1aed2c48b6146 lines:537 ===
001 # Touch Psychology Reference
002 
003 > Deep dive into mobile touch interaction, Fitts' Law for touch, thumb zone anatomy, gesture psychology, and haptic feedback.
004 > **This is the mobile equivalent of ux-psychology.md - CRITICAL for all mobile work.**
005 
006 ---
007 
008 ## 1. Fitts' Law for Touch
009 
010 ### The Fundamental Difference
011 
012 ```
013 DESKTOP (Mouse/Trackpad):
014 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Cursor size: 1 pixel (precision)
015 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Visual feedback: Hover states
016 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Error cost: Low (easy to retry)
017 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Target acquisition: Fast, precise
018 
019 MOBILE (Finger):
020 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Contact area: ~7mm diameter (imprecise)
021 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Visual feedback: No hover, only tap
022 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Error cost: High (frustrating retries)
023 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Occlusion: Finger covers the target
024 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Target acquisition: Slower, needs larger targets
025 ```
026 
027 ### Fitts' Law Formula Adapted
028 
029 ```
030 Touch acquisition time = a + b √ó log‚ÇÇ(1 + D/W)
031 
032 Where:
033 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ D = Distance to target
034 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ W = Width of target
035 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ For touch: W must be MUCH larger than desktop
036 ```
037 
038 ### Minimum Touch Target Sizes
039 
040 | Platform | Minimum | Recommended | Use For |
041 |----------|---------|-------------|---------|
042 | **iOS (HIG)** | 44pt √ó 44pt | 48pt+ | All tappable elements |
043 | **Android (Material)** | 48dp √ó 48dp | 56dp+ | All tappable elements |
044 | **WCAG 2.2** | 44px √ó 44px | - | Accessibility compliance |
045 | **Critical Actions** | - | 56-64px | Primary CTAs, destructive actions |
046 
047 ### Visual Size vs Hit Area
048 
049 ```
050 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
051 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
052 ‚îÇ    ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê      ‚îÇ
053 ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ                         ‚îÇ      ‚îÇ
054 ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ    [  BUTTON  ]         ‚îÇ ‚Üê Visual: 36px
055 ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ                         ‚îÇ      ‚îÇ
056 ‚îÇ    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò      ‚îÇ
057 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ ‚Üê Hit area: 48px (padding extends)
058 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
059 
060 ‚úÖ CORRECT: Visual can be smaller if hit area is minimum 44-48px
061 ‚ùå WRONG: Making hit area same as small visual element
062 ```
063 
064 ### Application Rules
065 
066 | Element | Visual Size | Hit Area |
067 |---------|-------------|----------|
068 | Icon buttons | 24-32px | 44-48px (padding) |
069 | Text links | Any | 44px height minimum |
070 | List items | Full width | 48-56px height |
071 | Checkboxes/Radio | 20-24px | 44-48px tap area |
072 | Close/X buttons | 24px | 44px minimum |
073 | Tab bar items | Icon 24-28px | Full tab width, 49px height (iOS) |
074 
075 ---
076 
077 ## 2. Thumb Zone Anatomy
078 
079 ### One-Handed Phone Usage
080 
081 ```
082 Research shows: 49% of users hold phone one-handed.
083 
084 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
085 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
086 ‚îÇ  ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê    ‚îÇ
087 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ       HARD TO REACH         ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ ‚Üê Status bar, top nav
088 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ      (requires stretch)     ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ    Put: Back, menu, settings
089 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ
090 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§    ‚îÇ
091 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ
092 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ       OK TO REACH           ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ ‚Üê Content area
093 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ      (comfortable)          ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ    Put: Secondary actions, content
094 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ
095 ‚îÇ  ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚î§    ‚îÇ
096 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ
097 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ       EASY TO REACH         ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ ‚Üê Tab bar, FAB zone
098 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ      (thumb's arc)          ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ    Put: PRIMARY CTAs!
099 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ                             ‚îÇ    ‚îÇ
100 ‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò    ‚îÇ
101 ‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ
102 ‚îÇ          [    HOME    ]             ‚îÇ
103 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
104 ```
105 
106 ### Thumb Arc (Right-Handed User)
107 
108 ```
109 Right hand holding phone:
110 
111 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
112 ‚îÇ  STRETCH      STRETCH    OK   ‚îÇ
113 ‚îÇ                               ‚îÇ
114 ‚îÇ  STRETCH        OK       EASY ‚îÇ
115 ‚îÇ                               ‚îÇ
116 ‚îÇ    OK          EASY      EASY ‚îÇ
117 ‚îÇ                               ‚îÇ
118 ‚îÇ   EASY         EASY      EASY ‚îÇ
119 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
120 
121 Left hand is mirrored.
122 ‚Üí Design for BOTH hands or assume right-dominant
123 ```
124 
125 ### Placement Guidelines
126 
127 | Element Type | Ideal Position | Reason |
128 |--------------|----------------|--------|
129 | **Primary CTA** | Bottom center/right | Easy thumb reach |
130 | **Tab bar** | Bottom | Natural thumb position |
131 | **FAB** | Bottom right | Easy for right hand |
132 | **Navigation** | Top (stretch) | Less frequent use |
133 | **Destructive actions** | Top left | Hard to reach = harder to accidentally tap |
134 | **Dismiss/Cancel** | Top left | Convention + safety |
135 | **Confirm/Done** | Top right or bottom | Convention |
136 
137 ### Large Phone Considerations (>6")
138 
139 ```
140 On large phones, top 40% becomes "dead zone" for one-handed use.
141 
142 Solutions:
143 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reachability features (iOS)
144 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Pull-down interfaces (drawer pulls content down)
145 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Bottom sheet navigation
146 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Floating action buttons
147 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Gesture-based alternatives to top actions
148 ```
149 
150 ---
151 
152 ## 3. Touch vs Click Psychology
153 
154 ### Expectation Differences
155 
156 | Aspect | Click (Desktop) | Touch (Mobile) |
157 |--------|-----------------|----------------|
158 | **Feedback timing** | Can wait 100ms | Expect instant (<50ms) |
159 | **Visual feedback** | Hover ‚Üí Click | Immediate tap response |
160 | **Error tolerance** | Easy retry | Frustrating, feels broken |
161 | **Precision** | High | Low |
162 | **Context menu** | Right-click | Long press |
163 | **Cancel action** | ESC key | Swipe away, outside tap |
164 
165 ### Touch Feedback Requirements
166 
167 ```
168 Tap ‚Üí Immediate visual change (< 50ms)
169 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Highlight state (background color change)
170 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Scale down slightly (0.95-0.98)
171 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Ripple effect (Android Material)
172 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Haptic feedback for confirmation
173 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Never nothing!
174 
175 Loading ‚Üí Show within 100ms
176 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ If action takes > 100ms
177 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Show spinner/progress
178 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Disable button (prevent double tap)
179 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Optimistic UI when possible
180 ```
181 
182 ### The "Fat Finger" Problem
183 
184 ```
185 Problem: Finger occludes target during tap
186 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User can't see exactly where they're tapping
187 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Visual feedback appears UNDER finger
188 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Increases error rate
189 
190 Solutions:
191 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Show feedback ABOVE touch point (tooltips)
192 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use cursor-like offset for precision tasks
193 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Magnification loupe for text selection
194 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Large enough targets that precision doesn't matter
195 ```
196 
197 ---
198 
199 ## 4. Gesture Psychology
200 
201 ### Gesture Discoverability Problem
202 
203 ```
204 Problem: Gestures are INVISIBLE.
205 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User must discover/remember them
206 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ No hover/visual hint
207 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Different mental model than tap
208 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Many users never discover gestures
209 
210 Solution: Always provide visible alternative
211 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Swipe to delete ‚Üí Also show delete button or menu
212 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Pull to refresh ‚Üí Also show refresh button
213 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Pinch to zoom ‚Üí Also show zoom controls
214 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Gestures as shortcuts, not only way
215 ```
216 
217 ### Common Gesture Conventions
218 
219 | Gesture | Universal Meaning | Usage |
220 |---------|-------------------|-------|
221 | **Tap** | Select, activate | Primary action |
222 | **Double tap** | Zoom in, like/favorite | Quick action |
223 | **Long press** | Context menu, selection mode | Secondary options |
224 | **Swipe horizontal** | Navigation, delete, actions | List actions |
225 | **Swipe down** | Refresh, dismiss | Pull to refresh |
226 | **Pinch** | Zoom in/out | Maps, images |
227 | **Two-finger scroll** | Scroll within scroll | Nested scrolls |
228 
229 ### Gesture Affordance Design
230 
231 ```
232 Swipe actions need visual hints:
233 
234 ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
235 ‚îÇ  ‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê                                  ‚îÇ
236 ‚îÇ  ‚îÇ ‚â° ‚îÇ  Item with hidden actions...   ‚Üí ‚îÇ ‚Üê Edge hint (partial color)
237 ‚îÇ  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò                                  ‚îÇ
238 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
239 
240 ‚úÖ Good: Slight color peek at edge suggesting swipe
241 ‚úÖ Good: Drag handle icon ( ‚â° ) suggesting reorder
242 ‚úÖ Good: Onboarding tooltip explaining gesture
243 ‚ùå Bad: Hidden gestures with no visual affordance
244 ```
245 
246 ### Platform Gesture Differences
247 
248 | Gesture | iOS | Android |
249 |---------|-----|---------|
250 | **Back** | Edge swipe from left | System back button/gesture |
251 | **Share** | Action sheet | Share sheet |
252 | **Context menu** | Long press / Force touch | Long press |
253 | **Dismiss modal** | Swipe down | Back button or swipe |
254 | **Delete in list** | Swipe left, tap delete | Swipe left, immediate or undo |
255 
256 ---
257 
258 ## 5. Haptic Feedback Patterns
259 
260 ### Why Haptics Matter
261 
262 ```
263 Haptics provide:
264 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Confirmation without looking
265 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Richer, more premium feel
266 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Accessibility (blind users)
267 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reduced error rate
268 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Emotional satisfaction
269 
270 Without haptics:
271 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Feels "cheap" or web-like
272 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User unsure if action registered
273 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Missed opportunity for delight
274 ```
275 
276 ### iOS Haptic Types
277 
278 | Type | Intensity | Use Case |
279 |------|-----------|----------|
280 | `selection` | Light | Picker scroll, toggle, selection |
281 | `light` | Light | Minor actions, hover equivalent |
282 | `medium` | Medium | Standard tap confirmation |
283 | `heavy` | Strong | Important completed, drop |
284 | `success` | Pattern | Task completed successfully |
285 | `warning` | Pattern | Warning, attention needed |
286 | `error` | Pattern | Error occurred |
287 
288 ### Android Haptic Types
289 
290 | Type | Use Case |
291 |------|----------|
292 | `CLICK` | Standard tap feedback |
293 | `HEAVY_CLICK` | Important actions |
294 | `DOUBLE_CLICK` | Confirm actions |
295 | `TICK` | Scroll/scrub feedback |
296 | `LONG_PRESS` | Long press activation |
297 | `REJECT` | Error/invalid action |
298 
299 ### Haptic Usage Guidelines
300 
301 ```
302 ‚úÖ DO use haptics for:
303 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Button taps
304 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Toggle switches
305 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Picker/slider values
306 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Pull to refresh trigger
307 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Successful action completion
308 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Errors and warnings
309 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Swipe action thresholds
310 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Important state changes
311 
312 ‚ùå DON'T use haptics for:
313 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Every scroll position
314 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Every list item
315 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Background events
316 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Passive displays
317 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Too frequently (haptic fatigue)
318 ```
319 
320 ### Haptic Intensity Mapping
321 
322 | Action Importance | Haptic Level | Example |
323 |-------------------|--------------|---------|
324 | Minor/Browsing | Light / None | Scrolling, hovering |
325 | Standard Action | Medium / Selection | Tap, toggle |
326 | Significant Action | Heavy / Success | Complete, confirm |
327 | Critical/Destructive | Heavy / Warning | Delete, payment |
328 | Error | Error pattern | Failed action |
329 
330 ---
331 
332 ## 6. Mobile Cognitive Load
333 
334 ### How Mobile Differs from Desktop
335 
336 | Factor | Desktop | Mobile | Implication |
337 |--------|---------|--------|-------------|
338 | **Attention** | Focused sessions | Interrupted constantly | Design for micro-sessions |
339 | **Context** | Controlled environment | Anywhere, any condition | Handle bad lighting, noise |
340 | **Multitasking** | Multiple windows | One app visible | Complete task in-app |
341 | **Input speed** | Fast (keyboard) | Slow (touch typing) | Minimize input, smart defaults |
342 | **Error recovery** | Easy (undo, back) | Harder (no keyboard shortcuts) | Prevent errors, easy recovery |
343 
344 ### Reducing Mobile Cognitive Load
345 
346 ```
347 1. ONE PRIMARY ACTION per screen
348    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Clear what to do next
349 
350 2. PROGRESSIVE DISCLOSURE
351    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Show only what's needed now
352 
353 3. SMART DEFAULTS
354    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Pre-fill what you can
355 
356 4. CHUNKING
357    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Break long forms into steps
358 
359 5. RECOGNITION over RECALL
360    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Show options, don't make user remember
361 
362 6. CONTEXT PERSISTENCE
363    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Save state on interrupt/background
364 ```
365 
366 ### Miller's Law for Mobile
367 
368 ```
369 Desktop: 7¬±2 items in working memory
370 Mobile: Reduce to 5¬±1 (more distractions)
371 
372 Navigation: Max 5 tab bar items
373 Options: Max 5 per menu level
374 Steps: Max 5 visible steps in progress
375 ```
376 
377 ### Hick's Law for Mobile
378 
379 ```
380 More choices = slower decisions
381 
382 Mobile impact: Even worse than desktop
383 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Smaller screen = less overview
384 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Scrolling required = items forgotten
385 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Interruptions = lost context
386 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Decision fatigue faster
387 
388 Solution: Progressive disclosure
389 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Start with 3-5 options
390 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ "More" for additional
391 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Smart ordering (most used first)
392 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Previous selections remembered
393 ```
394 
395 ---
396 
397 ## 7. Touch Accessibility
398 
399 ### Motor Impairment Considerations
400 
401 ```
402 Users with motor impairments may:
403 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Have tremors (need larger targets)
404 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Use assistive devices (different input method)
405 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Have limited reach (one-handed necessity)
406 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Need more time (avoid timeouts)
407 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Make accidental touches (need confirmation)
408 
409 Design responses:
410 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Generous touch targets (48dp+)
411 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Adjustable timing for gestures
412 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Undo for destructive actions
413 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Switch control support
414 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Voice control support
415 ```
416 
417 ### Touch Target Spacing (A11y)
418 
419 ```
420 WCAG 2.2 Success Criterion 2.5.8:
421 
422 Touch targets MUST have:
423 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Width: ‚â• 44px
424 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Height: ‚â• 44px
425 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Spacing: ‚â• 8px from adjacent targets
426 
427 OR the target is:
428 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Inline (within text)
429 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ User-controlled (user can resize)
430 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Essential (no alternative design)
431 ```
432 
433 ### Accessible Touch Patterns
434 
435 | Pattern | Accessible Implementation |
436 |---------|---------------------------|
437 | Swipe actions | Provide menu alternative |
438 | Drag and drop | Provide select + move option |
439 | Pinch zoom | Provide zoom buttons |
440 | Force touch | Provide long press alternative |
441 | Shake gesture | Provide button alternative |
442 
443 ---
444 
445 ## 8. Emotion in Touch
446 
447 ### The Premium Feel
448 
449 ```
450 What makes touch feel "premium":
451 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Instant response (< 50ms)
452 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Appropriate haptic feedback
453 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Smooth 60fps animations
454 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Correct resistance/physics
455 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Sound feedback (when appropriate)
456 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Attention to spring physics
457 ```
458 
459 ### Emotional Touch Feedback
460 
461 | Emotion | Touch Response |
462 |---------|----------------|
463 | Success | Haptic success + confetti/check |
464 | Error | Haptic error + shake animation |
465 | Warning | Haptic warning + attention color |
466 | Delight | Unexpected smooth animation |
467 | Power | Heavy haptic on significant action |
468 
469 ### Trust Building Through Touch
470 
471 ```
472 Trust signals in touch interactions:
473 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Consistent behavior (same action = same response)
474 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Reliable feedback (never fails silently)
475 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Secure feel for sensitive actions
476 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Professional animations (not janky)
477 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ No accidental actions (confirmation for destructive)
478 ```
479 
480 ---
481 
482 ## 9. Touch Psychology Checklist
483 
484 ### Before Every Screen
485 
486 - [ ] **All touch targets ‚â• 44-48px?**
487 - [ ] **Primary CTA in thumb zone?**
488 - [ ] **Destructive actions require confirmation?**
489 - [ ] **Gesture alternatives exist (visible buttons)?**
490 - [ ] **Haptic feedback on important actions?**
491 - [ ] **Immediate visual feedback on tap?**
492 - [ ] **Loading states for actions > 100ms?**
493 
494 ### Before Release
495 
496 - [ ] **Tested on smallest supported device?**
497 - [ ] **Tested one-handed on large phone?**
498 - [ ] **All gestures have visible alternatives?**
499 - [ ] **Haptics work correctly (test on device)?**
500 - [ ] **Touch targets tested with accessibility settings?**
501 - [ ] **No tiny close buttons or icons?**
502 
503 ---
504 
505 ## 10. Quick Reference Card
506 
507 ### Touch Target Sizes
508 
509 ```
510                      iOS        Android     WCAG
511 Minimum:           44pt       48dp       44px
512 Recommended:       48pt+      56dp+      -
513 Spacing:           8pt+       8dp+       8px+
514 ```
515 
516 ### Thumb Zone Actions
517 
518 ```
519 TOP:      Navigation, settings, back (infrequent)
520 MIDDLE:   Content, secondary actions
521 BOTTOM:   Primary CTA, tab bar, FAB (frequent)
522 ```
523 
524 ### Haptic Selection
525 
526 ```
527 Light:    Selection, toggle, minor
528 Medium:   Tap, standard action
529 Heavy:    Confirm, complete, drop
530 Success:  Task done
531 Error:    Failed action
532 Warning:  Attention needed
533 ```
534 
535 ---
536 
537 > **Remember:** Every touch is a conversation between user and device. Make it feel natural, responsive, and respectful of human fingers‚Äînot precise cursor points.

006 
007 # Next.js Best Practices
008 
009 > Principles for Next.js App Router development.
010 
011 ---
012 
013 ## 1. Server vs Client Components
014 
015 ### Decision Tree
016 
017 ```
018 Does it need...?
019 ‚îÇ
020 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ useState, useEffect, event handlers
021 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Client Component ('use client')
022 ‚îÇ
023 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Direct data fetching, no interactivity
024 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Server Component (default)
025 ‚îÇ
026 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Both?
027     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Split: Server parent + Client child
028 ```
029 
030 ### By Default
031 
032 | Type | Use |
033 |------|-----|
034 | **Server** | Data fetching, layout, static content |
035 | **Client** | Forms, buttons, interactive UI |
036 
037 ---
038 
039 ## 2. Data Fetching Patterns
040 
041 ### Fetch Strategy
042 
043 | Pattern | Use |
044 |---------|-----|
045 | **Default** | Static (cached at build) |
046 | **Revalidate** | ISR (time-based refresh) |
047 | **No-store** | Dynamic (every request) |
048 
049 ### Data Flow
050 
051 | Source | Pattern |
052 |--------|---------|
053 | Database | Server Component fetch |
054 | API | fetch with caching |
055 | User input | Client state + server action |
056 
057 ---
058 
059 ## 3. Routing Principles
060 
061 ### File Conventions
062 
063 | File | Purpose |
064 |------|---------|
065 | `page.tsx` | Route UI |
066 | `layout.tsx` | Shared layout |
067 | `loading.tsx` | Loading state |
068 | `error.tsx` | Error boundary |
069 | `not-found.tsx` | 404 page |
070 
071 ### Route Organization
072 
073 | Pattern | Use |
074 |---------|-----|
075 | Route groups `(name)` | Organize without URL |
076 | Parallel routes `@slot` | Multiple same-level pages |
077 | Intercepting `(.)` | Modal overlays |
078 
079 ---
080 
081 ## 4. API Routes
082 
083 ### Route Handlers
084 
085 | Method | Use |
086 |--------|-----|
087 | GET | Read data |
088 | POST | Create data |
089 | PUT/PATCH | Update data |
090 | DELETE | Remove data |
091 
092 ### Best Practices
093 
094 - Validate input with Zod
095 - Return proper status codes
096 - Handle errors gracefully
097 - Use Edge runtime when possible
098 
099 ---
100 
101 ## 5. Performance Principles
102 
103 ### Image Optimization
104 
105 - Use next/image component
106 - Set priority for above-fold
107 - Provide blur placeholder
108 - Use responsive sizes
109 
110 ### Bundle Optimization
111 
112 - Dynamic imports for heavy components
113 - Route-based code splitting (automatic)
114 - Analyze with bundle analyzer
115 
116 ---
117 
118 ## 6. Metadata
119 
120 ### Static vs Dynamic
121 
122 | Type | Use |
123 |------|-----|
124 | Static export | Fixed metadata |
125 | generateMetadata | Dynamic per-route |
126 
127 ### Essential Tags
128 
129 - title (50-60 chars)
130 - description (150-160 chars)
131 - Open Graph images
132 - Canonical URL
133 
134 ---
135 
136 ## 7. Caching Strategy
137 
138 ### Cache Layers
139 
140 | Layer | Control |
141 |-------|---------|
142 | Request | fetch options |
143 | Data | revalidate/tags |
144 | Full route | route config |
145 
146 ### Revalidation
147 
148 | Method | Use |
149 |--------|-----|
150 | Time-based | `revalidate: 60` |
151 | On-demand | `revalidatePath/Tag` |
152 | No cache | `no-store` |
153 
154 ---
155 
156 ## 8. Server Actions
157 
158 ### Use Cases
159 
160 - Form submissions
161 - Data mutations
162 - Revalidation triggers
163 
164 ### Best Practices
165 
166 - Mark with 'use server'
167 - Validate all inputs
168 - Return typed responses
169 - Handle errors
170 
171 ---
172 
173 ## 9. Anti-Patterns
174 
175 | ‚ùå Don't | ‚úÖ Do |
176 |----------|-------|
177 | 'use client' everywhere | Server by default |
178 | Fetch in client components | Fetch in server |
179 | Skip loading states | Use loading.tsx |
180 | Ignore error boundaries | Use error.tsx |
181 | Large client bundles | Dynamic imports |
182 
183 ---
184 
185 ## 10. Project Structure
186 
187 ```
188 app/
189 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ (marketing)/     # Route group
190 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ page.tsx
191 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ (dashboard)/
192 ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ layout.tsx   # Dashboard layout
193 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ page.tsx
194 ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ api/
195 ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ [resource]/
196 ‚îÇ       ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ route.ts
197 ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ components/
198     ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ ui/
199 ```
200 
201 ---
202 
203 > **Remember:** Server Components are the default for a reason. Start there, add client only when needed.
